PAGE: "Talva Silvertongue"
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/"Talva_Silvertongue"
======================================================================

For information on the real Talva, see
Talva Silvertongue
.
"Talva Silvertongue"
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Crimsonblade
Occupation
Pirate
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
"Talva Silvertongue"
is an
NPC
in
Diablo Immortal
.
Biography
"Talva" was a member of the
Crimsonblade
, who impersonated the real
Talva Silvertongue
as part of the Crimsonblades' scam to pass off their
haven
as
Port Justinian
, after luring in ship captains.
Things went awry with the arrival of
Roul Terrago
, or more specifically, a
hero/group of heroes
who arrived at the same time. They tried to convince Roul that this wasn't Port Justinian, but he didn't listen to them. "Talva" escorted Roul to his cabin, while setting his pirates on the interloper(s).
Inside the cabin of the pirates'
ship
, Roul became more suspicious, and "Talva" lost patience. He ordered his men to take Roul away, while he and his men fought the hero(es). However, "Talva" was killed, and Roul saved.
In-game
"Talva" in-game
"Talva" appears in
Crimsonblade Haven
during the "
Broken Compass
"
side quest
. He is an NPC in this stage of the quest, but later appears as a
Super Unique
monster
on Rhodri's Ship, where he is fought inside the ship's cabin. His attack pattern appears similar to
Rhodri the Red
.
Quotes
"Master Roul, please don't be fooled by the local scoundrels. They'll cheat you as soon as soon as your eyelids drop. Come, allow me to escort you to my cabin so that we can discuss the...delivery of your cargo."
(upon being encountered)
"Boys! Deal with this interloper, please."
"Damn you! You just had to stick your nose where it doesn't belong. The jig's up, boys. Gut them!"
(at the start of the fight)
"Come on, boys! Show this meddler no mercy!"
Combat
"Talva Silvertongue" uses the following skills; a melee slash and a ranged empowered slash that sends out a wave of force.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
"Talva's" in-game model is basically a pallette-swapped version of
Rhodri the Red
, with him having green clothes and brown hair instead of red clothes and black hair. His attacks share the same animations (if not effects) with Rhodri.
Image

Acolyte of Damnation
Gender

Cult of Damnation
Class
High Priest of Damnation

Status

Appearances
Diablo Immortal
The
Acolyte of Damnation
was a member of the
Cult of Damnation
.
In
1270
, he and his
fellow cultists
abducted a number of townsfolk from
Wortham
, bringing them to the
Vile Refuge
. Many of them were sacrificed to the "Lord of Damnation" before a
hero/group of heroes
arrived, finding only a few survivors left. The Acolyte appeared and confronted them, and while he was defeated, it was not before he killed two of the three remaining villagers.
In-game
The Acolyte of Damnation is a super unique
Damned Summoner
boss
seen toward the start of
Diablo Immortal
. He is fought in the Vile Refuge.
The fight occurs in two phases. At the end of the first one, the Acolyte summons
Hellions
, while engaging with the player(s) by attacking them from range, and
teleporting
. At the start of the second one, he will summon
Acolyte's Shadows
.
Quotes

your
flesh the

shall have its prize!

Hell's
new master!
(at the start of the second phase of the boss fight)

Adrahau
is an
NPC

.
Lore
Adrahau was a
witch
of one of the
Witch Circles
of the
Sharval Wilds
at the time when the
Voidwound
was first unleashed. A notable feat of hers are the shackles she made which can bind
powerful
demons
, even at their full strength.
These shackles were used to bind the Voidwound before they were sealed
, and long after her death; the Howling Terror
.
Legacy
"You are not permitted here. In the names of Adrahau and Gwerith, be bound"
- Nisza
(
src
)
Because of her contribution in the sealing of the Voidwound, Adrahau's name was well respected, and some witches even prayed in her name.

Aisah
Gender

Appearances

Aisah
was a member of the
Cult of Damnation
.
Biography
Aisah played a pocket lyre.
In/around
1270
, Aisah and her daughter,
Luzja
, were on
Mount Zavain
, along with
Razmus
,
Omer
, and
Laksmi
. Laksmi noted that Aisah seemed off, and her suspicions were well-founded as Aisah handed over her fellow travellers to the cult (she also apparently intended on handing over Luzjah as well). Aisah left with
Vizibor
, who empowered her in a ritual, as Aisah had proven her dedication to the cult. However, she was slain almost immediately afterwards by an
adventurer
. Her pocket lyre was returned to Luzja, who was kept ignorant as to how far into darkness Aisah had fallen.
In-game
Aisah appears as a
Super Unique Monster
in
Diablo Immortal
in the
side quest
"
The Bond
." She is a
Damned Cultist
, but bereft of any special properties.

Akinees
Title
The Throne-Lashed
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Cult of Terror
Class
Deadwright
Occupation
Priest
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
Akinees the Throne-Lashed
is a member of
Cult of Terror
that attacked
Stormpoint Keep
and its leader.
Lore
Akinees has faithfully served his
master
as the current leader of the Cult of Terror.
Around
1272
, he led the Cult of Terror to besiege
Stormpoint
after a shard of the
Worldstone
had been divined to be on the island. As they could not divine the precise location of the shard, he ordered them to storm the island with demonic reinforcements, killing any opposition they encounter and using the survivors for
haruspex
.
At a point, he invited the
Bride of Hell
to inspect his progress, but was interrupted by scrying on their location. Unfortunately the strangers got away.
Impatient with the progress of the search, he summoned the
Howling Terror
to hunt the shard from the skies.
The cult made a base in
the Planks
, and Akinees resided in a
Tidal Cavern
beneath the base. Here, captured villagers from
the Shanties
were delivered to him for sacrifice. Unfortunately
the Shard-seeker
found him and was able to drive him off.
Akinees, with the shard at last
Unknown to the Shard-seeker, Akinees kept track of their progress through divination. Once they retrieved the shard from the
Warden's pet
, he sent cultists to attack children under the Shard-seeker's protection. Using that distraction, he stole the shard and portaled away.
In-game
Dialogue box portrait of Akinees
Akinees is the first
boss
encountered in the
Terror's Tide
storyline of
Diablo Immortal
. He is fought in the
Tidal Cavern
at the end of
The Planks
. Hecan
teleport
, summon parts of big
Demon
and electric orbs. After his defeat, he escapes through a portal.
He makes other appearances at later points in the storyline, appearing in the quest
Bound for Eternity
. He is also featured in the
Destruction's Wake
update, in the quests
My Father's House
and
Creation's Husk
.
At the end of the latter,he is featured as a mini-boss where he is killed.
Quotes
"They are more in death then they ever were in life."
"May depths claim you all."
"Fear guides your every move."
"You seek to frighten me, more than the
Lord of Terror
himself?
I will show you fear."
(after being threatened by
the Shard-seeker
)
"
Great One
! Ease from your throne and burn the sky black."
(Summoning Shumbeel to battle the Shard-seeker)
Gallery
From L-R; Akinees,
Bride of Hell
and
Viv Mesztros
Akinees summons Shumbeel for a final showdown with the Shard-seeker

angels
and

. I will strengthen your flesh...make you powerful, glorious

. Fear not. We will liberate this
world
. Those blind to our future will be made to see. Rejoice! We shall be free!"
- Albrecht
(src)
Albrecht
Title
The First Shardborne
The Shardborne Prophet
Mad Prince of Freedom
Gender
Male
Race
Human
(formerly)
Shardborne
Affiliation
Khanduras
(formerly)
Cult of Terror
(formerly)
Shardborne
Class
Shardborne (Fleshwarped)

's servant (formerly)

(father),

(mother)

Diablo

Crimson Mass
The Order

Deckard Cain's Journal

Book of Cain
(mentioned only)
Book of Tyrael
Greatest of Kings
Prince Albrecht of Khanduras
was the younger son of King
Leoric
and Queen
Asylla
. Once possessed by
Diablo
, he became a leader of the
Shardborne
.
Biography
Early Life
Albrecht was born into light and love.
He accompanied his family when they came to
Tristram
, from where Leoric would govern
Khanduras
. Leoric noted that Albrecht appeared to enjoy his new home.
Albrecht would occasionally take swordfighting lessons from
Aidan
when the latter had time to spare. At a point he tried to fight a group of direwolves to show his progress, but had to be saved by Aidan after being overwhelmed.
Albrecht dreamt of being a great king.
The Darkening of Tristram
"And a child will cradle
Terror
in his breast as the heart of
man
falls under the shadow."
-
Prophecies of the Final Day
(excerpt)
(
src
)
As the
Darkening of Tristram
progressed,
Diablo
attempted to claim the king's body, but was not strong enough to fully take possession. The
demon
required a host, simple and innocent, and thus found Albrecht to be fitting.
Diablo possesses Albrecht
Albrecht was captured by the traitorous
Archbishop Lazarus
and was taken down into the depths of the catacombs of the
Tristram Cathedral
.
There, Albrecht was set free and allowed to flee in terror. Diablo's spirit haunted him as he ran through the labyrinth until he came to a dead end. In the height of his terror,
Albrecht was recaptured and Diablo's shattered
soulstone
was driven into Albrecht's forehead, and the Lord of Terror's vile spirit possessed him and eventually twisted the boy's body into an approximation of his true form.
A group of heroes—
Jazreth
,
a Vizjerei sorcerer
,
Moreina
the
Rogue
captain, and Albrecht's older brother, Prince
Aidan
—entered the darkened monastery in an attempt to find and rescue the young Prince. Lazarus was encountered and defeated at the
Unholy Altar
, but the adventurers only found a different child, sacrificed by Lazarus as an offering.
Unwilling to give up hope, the heroes sought out, encountered, and eventually vanquished the Lord of Terror himself. Diablo let out a tortured scream of death, which went all the way up to the mortal realm, shattering the windows of the cathedral. In his dreams,
Deckard Cain
could have sworn that he heard a child's scream in the midst of the terrible roar.
Kneeling down beside the defeated
Prime Evil
, Aidan used a small blade to remove the soulstone from Diablo's forehead. The demon's body transformed back into that of Prince Albrecht, who then gasped his final breaths.
Dark Rebirth
Albrecht, reborn as a Shardborne
Fourteen years later
, the
Cult of Terror
returned to Tristram. Their plan; to use the imprints of Diablo's former host and lair - Albrecht and the
Tristram Cathedral
, respectively - to perform a ritual that would create a path to their master. Traces of Albrecht's
essence
was harvested
his childhood home
from sentimental objects of his childhood and stored in a
Worldstone
shard. In a ritual within the depths of the cathedral, the
Bride of Hell
channeled energy from the shard into Albrecht's
corpse
, and his memories were projected as
a separate plane
.
The mixture of his essence and power of Creation suffusing his corpse resurrected Albrecht and transformed him into a into a
Shardborne
.
Albrecht rose with the voice of the boy he was, fragmented mind and an ever—shifting physicality.
He then fought against
the Shard-seeker
, who was pursuing the Bride. Albrecht was defeated, but spared as his opponent was in a hurry. Within his projected memories, the Bride created a path to Diablo using memory containing the strongest imprint of the demon (the moment Albrecht was possessed) and she was able to open a portal to her master and deliver the shard to him.
Splintered Souls
"The voices make you strong. You can be stronger. Follow me."
- Albrecht to other
Shardborne
(
src
)
Some time later, shortly after the Shard-seeker left the
Southern Dreadlands
, Albrecht was seen leading other
Shardborne
to the
Gully of Madness
.
Albrecht gathered many Worldstone splinters from the gully
and became the primary voice in the Chorus of Shardborne.
His mind and body stabilized as a (implied) result.
Sanctuary's Unmaking
After Diablo was fully restored he used his Worldstone shard to bring all Shardborne under his control.
Albrecht was tasked with guarding one of the portals
that transported darkness from
the Black Spire
to other parts of the island. Albrecht faced the Shard-seeker again, but was no match for them as they were boosted by
El'druin
. Even power granted by Diablo couldn't secure victory. On the verge of defeat Albrecht begged for more power, but Diablo answered with silence. The Shard-seeker's hesitation to kill Albrecht gave him the chance to escape through the portal.
The Bargain for Freedom
"...While He has the stone, we are all slaves. There are only two options: redemption or freedom. I could trade you for the former... but perhaps you're willing to make a bargain of your own?
I want to be free of His voice. I want you to kill Terror. Could you reach him with your shattered army? And what would you ask in return?"
- Albrecht
(
src
)
Albrecht chaffed under Diablo's leash and he saw a chance for freedom in the Shard-seeker. However, he needed to wait for a situation where they will be forced to listen.
Albrecht gifts the Shard-seeker an eye
The Protectors of Sanctuary were decimated by the Song of Unmaking
and the survivors retreated to an
Underground Camp
in the
Tar Wells
.
Epoch of Madness
"Diablo has been driven back, and a massive shard of the Worldstone has been destroyed at last. The risen prince Albrecht, son of King Leoric, and one-time host of Terror, is now free from demonic control. He's led his Shardborne family to a new home. A place of venerated kings and ancient wilderness. But does he arrive as a destroyer...or a savior?"
-
Ryan Quinn
(src)
With Diablo's defeat at
World's Crown
, Albrecht was freed from the Lord of Terror's influence. He led the Shardborne (whom he now considered family) into the
Sharval Wilds
, which he intended to be their new home.

Flesh Harvest
Albrecht leads the Shardborne
Within the
Boil of Creation
, Albrecht planned to transform Sanctuary in his own image,
and build a kingdom the Shardborne could call their own. During this period, he further empowered himself, creating new Shardborne.
This section is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
The First and Last King
Albrecht
The destruction of the Boil sent Albrecht even further down the dark path he trod. Maddened by loss and betrayal, and with the energy of the Worldstone that suffused him growing ever more unstable,
Albrecht marched with his twisted legions through the
towns
of Sharval with powerful Shardborne bolstering his ranks. After the loss of his twisted paradise, Albrecht lead legions of new Shardborne through the populous areas of
Entsteig
. He personally created
the Fleshwarped
Shardborne,
and sought to claim Entsteig as his own.
If he could not create a kingdom for the Shardborne, he would take Entsteig as his own kingdom.
However, he was defeated.
This section is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
In-game
Diablo I
Albrecht is seen in the ending cinematic of
Diablo
, though has no actual in-game presence.
Diablo Immortal
This section is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
Personality and Traits
Albrecht
While once a timid child, Albrecht's demeanor darkened as a Shardborne. Warped and reborn by the power of the Worldstone,
he saw the Shardborne as his family,
and as the future of
humanity
.
Despite this, Albrecht carried some of his old yearnings to deliver a common good, and for a family he barely had time to know. The destruction of the Boil of Creation drove him even further from the child he used to be.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
Albrecht is the only known host for any
Prime Evil
to transform into human form and/or remain alive (even for a few moments) after the defeat of the possessing demon.
Albrecht's boss form in
Tristram Cathedral
dungeon
is titled "The First Shardborne." While he is the first named Shardborne encountered in the franchise, the
Splintered Souls
update reveals that Shardborne have existed around the
Southern Dreadlands
since
the destruction
of the
Worldstone
.

"Potion dealer who would rather be somewhere else. He is pleasant, but seems distracted, perhaps even bored- always reading a book and mumbling strange words."
- Character description
(src)
Alkor
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Occupation
Potion dealer
Alchemist
Status
Active (as of
1264
)
Appearances
Diablo II
To Hell and Back
Alkor
was a potion-dealer who resided in
Kurast
.
Alkor was loathe to be interrupted or disturbed, but if one managed to get his attention, he did his best to aid them for as long as his battered wits allow him to remain focused. He was interested in
Necromancers
,
and maintained a grimoire, along with a library of
tomes
—
heretical
,
exegetical
,
hermeneutical
, and
pharmaceutical
.
Biography
By
1264
, Alkor was already a model of old age, with a balding head, flowing grey beard, and a gnarled old staff. He reeked of unwashed sweat and "other odors best left unsaid."
As Kurast came under assault by
demons
, Alkor had good business with
Asheara
, who 'bought' a "potion of manliness" from him every week." He had no such luck with
Natalya
, however.
When a
group of heroes
came to Kurast in pursuit of the
Dark Wanderer
, he aided them in their goals.
In-game
Alkor
Appears in
Diablo II
Significance
Minor
Service(s)
gossip,
Gamble
and
Trade
services,
Quest
initiation
Residence(s)
Kurast Docks
Starts quest(s)
Lam Esen's Tome (quest)
Portrayed by
Brian George
Alkor is an NPC from
Diablo II
,
Act III
. He is an alchemist, similar to
Lysander
in personality and wares. Alkor's shop is at the top of the map, where he sells various potions. He is also very fond of
necromancers
. Apparently, he has a number of odd potions, claiming that
Asheara
is a good customer as she buys a "potion of manliness" from him every week, although the latter is most likely Alkor's rude sense of humor.
He also claims to have a library of  tomes. The pharmaceutical tomes would make sense for an alchemist, while the rest concern religious texts, which explains why Alkor is familiar with
Lam Esen's Tome
.

Introduction
General
Damn it, I wish you people would just leave me alone! I...
Oh, you're new here, aren't you?
I am Alkor, the Alchemist. I dabble in potions and salves, and I can sell you some if you really need them.
But don't make a habit of coming here. I don't like to be disturbed while I'm studying!
Necromancer
Damn it, I wish you people would just leave me alone! I...
Oh, you're a Necromancer, aren't you? I've heard that your kind use powerful potions and such to wake the dead and control spirits. I'd love to discuss what components you use some time.
I am Alkor, the Alchemist. I dabble in potions and salves, myself, and I can sell you some if you really need them.
...Feel free to drop by anytime.

Badgering

Ormus
Oh, Ormus has been talking in riddles for years. I think he does it to cover up the fact that he's got nothing intelligent to say.
Natalya

Evil (Necromancer)

Golden Bird (Cut)

The Golden Bird
Quest Initiation
Many alchemists believe that Ku Y'leh's magical elixirs bonded with his body before his death. His ashes are, therefore, considered to be very rare, highly potent alchemical ingredients. If I could procure the ashes, I would create a potion which could defy death itself!
After Initiate
Remember, Ku Y'leh's ashes are stored within the statuette of the Golden Bird. The bird is worth a great deal to the one who can locate it.

Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
Alkor had a very strong Indian accent.
Alkor's line "I hope you don't object to my badgering the witless" is a pun on the legal concept of
badgering the witness
.
Alkor's reference to a "Potion of Manliness", may imply that he was in a relationship with
Asheara
, if this is indeed the case, Asheara herself makes no reference to it.
Alkor the Snow Leopard
is presumably named after him.

PAGE: Alyssa
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Alyssa
======================================================================

Alyssa
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Affiliation
Blackstone Village
Relatives
Lucian
(father)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
Alyssa
was the daughter of
Lucian
.
Biography
Alyssa and her father resided in the
town
of
Blackstone Village
. In
1270
, it was attacked by the
Bloodsworn
. Lucian told her to stay hidden, while he went to find help. He promised that he would come back to save her. She hid herself in their house's cellar, but the cellar door was blocked by rubble. Terrified, she called out for her father, and caught the attention of some of the
Bloodsworn
. However, the cultists were killed by a
hero/group of heroes
, who promptly removed the rubble, allowing Alyssa to climb out.
Unfortunately, the hero(es) informed Alyssa that her father was dead, and that his last request had been to deliver a
letter
to someone named
Kashya
. Alyssa refused to believe them at first, but eventually accepted her father's
death
. She departed with the hero(es) to find the
Sisterhood of the Sightless Eye
. However, they didn't get far before they were attacked by more Bloodsworn. The cultists were slain, but while Alyssa wasn't wounded physically, her emotional wounds were weighing her down. She explained how one of the Bloodsworn women had taunted her, as if she was nothing...and now, she was the only survivor of her village. The hero(es) reassured Alyssa that she wasn't worthless, and that the Bloodsworn would pay for what they did. But for that to happen, they had to find Kashya.
Alyssa's body
It was at this moment that vines erupted from the ground, incapacitating Alyssa. More Bloodsworn attacked, but they were repelled, in part due to Kashya and her fellow
Rogues
. However, Alyssa didn't survive, much to the grief of her would-be rescuers.
In-game
Alyssa is an
NPC
in
Diablo Immortal
. She is found in Blackstone Village, during the "
Lucian's Hope
"
quest
.

PAGE: Amelia Cain
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Amelia_Cain
======================================================================

Amelia Cain
Gender
Female
Relatives
Deckard Cain
(husband)
Jered Cain
(son)
Aderes Cain
(mother in-law)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
The Order
(flashback only)
Amelia Cain
was the wife of
Deckard Cain
.
Biography
Closure for the Betrothed
"Deckard, promise me you'll be careful. Even if this artifact is what you think, it's not worth risking your life. Your mother wouldn't want that for you."
- Amelia to Deckard, just before the latter leaves in search of the vault
(
src
)
Portrait of the Cain family
While Amelia was still betrothed to Deckard,
Aderes Cain
—her mother in-law—died in a summer c.
late 1220's
. For years after that, Amelia took a white bouquet of Aderes' favorite flowers to her grave on every anniversary in order to pay her respects.
Deckard and Amelia pay their respects at Aderes' grave
A few years later,
Basim
; an old friend of Cain, came to her husband with news of an interesting artifact. The artifact supposedly could summon the spirit of the deceased, and was a chance for Deckard to find closure for his mother's death. Aderes' anniversary came soon after, and while Amelia was on her way to the florist, she met an adventurer looking for her husband for help in translating a tome. She invited them to accompany her to the cemetery where Cain was. She got her flowers and the 2 met Cain at the cemetery. After paying their respects, they returned home with their guest for Cain to hear their request. Cain agreed to help the adventurer if they help him on his quest to acquire the artifact. Before they left, Amelia expressed her concern to her husband and made him promise to be careful.
Cain returned with a mirror, but was stumped on how to activate it. He has an argument with Basim, after which the latter left. Basim returned months later, claiming to have found a clue in activating the mirror. Amelia was worried about their actions because she thought that they were meddling with forces that ought not be meddled with. Furthermore, Basim seemed desperate for them to succeed, as though it was his own mother that was to be summoned.
Love through the Dark
"Please, you're scaring me."
"You should be scared. I will feast on this world!"
"Deckard, look at me. It's Amelia, your betrothed!"
- Amelia and a possessed Deckard
(
src
)
Amelia tries to return Cain to his senses
The adventure returned around this time, and the duo went to the cemetery where Deckard and Basim went to perform the ritual. They arrived just in time to see Deckard be possessed by the mirror, and Basim reveal himself to be a cultist. The adventurer protected her, and defeated Basim and his cultists. The possessed Deckard then tried to summon
undead
, but Amelia ran to him and hugged him. She was able to bring him to his senses by calling her name, and Deckard banished
the malicious force
from his body.
Childbirth and Death
In
1233
, she gave birth to her son,
Jered
. Jered's name however, was a point of contention that added to the growing tension between her and her husband. Cain was far too focused on his studies and role as
Tristram
's schoolmaster for Amelia's liking. Why had he named Jered after his
famous ancestor
, she asked, when Deckard's
Horadric
lineage supposedly meant nothing to him? And why was he never there for his son, or for her?
Four years after Jered's birth, the strain in the marriage came to a head, and Amelia up and left Tristram and Deckard, taking Jered with her. They headed east, with the intent of living with her mother. However, bandits attacked their wagon, and both Amelia and her son were killed.
Thomas Abbey
's
men
suspected that they had been killed by bandits, but the perpetrators were never found.
Legacy
Cain shows the portrait of his family to Karshun and the Shard-seeker
The deaths of his wife and son haunted Deckard decades after their death, and he still held onto the death notice he had received concerning them. He kept a portrait of himself with Amelia and an infant Jered, as it was the last thing he had of them, save memories.
Years later
,
Belial
turned Cain's grief against him. Twisting the truth as per his wont as the Lord of Lies, Belial claimed that Jered and his mother were actually attacked by
khazra
, their souls dragged down into the
Burning Hells
to writhe in agony. In the end though, Deckard saw through his lies.

PAGE: Amolia
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Amolia
======================================================================

Amolia
was one of the spellcasters in service of the 'enforcing arm' of the ruling
Council of Clans
. Along with
Kethuus
and
Nurzani
, she was dispatched by the Council to track down the fugitive mage
Zorun Tzin
.
Amolia was eventually possessed by the specter
Malic
, who used her body to get into contact with the Council of Clans - after which he murdered everyone of them. Though Amolia's spirit was already gone by then, her body was eventually destroyed when Malic found a new host - the unsuspecting priestess,
Oris
.
Personality and Traits
Amolia was
Ascenian
, so had much lighter skin than
Kehjistani
. Her face bore a startling similarity with that of
Lylia
, the human guise of the demoness
Lilith
. Like many mages, she was haughty, egocentric, and overconfident of her abilities.

. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by

PAGE: Angmet
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Angmet
======================================================================

Agmet
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Class
Alchemist
Occupation
Apprentice Alchemist (formerly)
Fireworks vendor
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Agmet
was a burgeoning alchemist known for his invention of fireworks.
Biography
Angmet started as an orphan apprenticing under an
alchemist
. Though he had little talent for alchemy, he proved dependable and thus was able to earn his keep.
One day, a basic remedy he tried to prepare instead formed a chalky, blackened stone. As Angmet disposed of it in the hearth, the most peculiar thing happened. It began to spark and leap about.
This discovery fascinated Angmet. As he experimented with it, he found ways to change the flame's color, make the stones crackle and dance in different ways. He sold his "fire-works" in his master's shop, and word soon spread.
In a few years time, Angmet had saved enough to open a shop next to his master's. There he sold amusements which produced entrancing effects when set aflame, each more elaborate than the last.
With Angmet's fame came pride. Hoping to expand his business, he sought to buy his master's shop. Angmet's master was not impressed by his pupil's success, but instead urged Angmet to rededicate himself to his studies.
This made Angmet to become spiteful of his master. He obsessed over the creation of more and more elaborate fireworks, hoping that if his achievements grew large enough, his master would have no choice but to recognize them.
At last, Angmet completed his masterwork, the "Everlasting Flame." Just as he had hoped, it burned without cease. Yet joy soon turned to despair as the Flame set Angmet and his store ablaze.
Terrible howls filled the street as Angmet's flesh sizzled and
burned
. The people of the city tried for days to tame the
inferno
, but like his ambition, Angmet could not be extinguished.
In-game
Agmet is mentioned in
Diablo Immortal
, in the flavor-text of the pieces of
Angmet's Conflagration
item set.

that came to aid of

when it was invaded by the

Biography
When the Cult of Terror was close to breaching the
Stormpoint Battlement
, a stranger came to the defenders aid, killing half dozen cultists without breaking a sweat. After they let him in, he asked the
commander
for a way into the
Abandoned Prison
. The commander refused, so Zatham began to plan a strategy to attack the cult and stop their advancement to the prison.
Luckily,
another adventurer
came to Stormpoint's rescue, also looking for a way into the prison. Grateful for the assistance, he told the Shard-seeker to stop the cultists from advancing through the sea while he would go after their aerial reinforcement. After that, he jumps through a portal to go after the
Howling Terror
as it was flying by.
Zatham meets the Shard-seeker again in the Warden's office just after a

in its rampage over it's
master's

its lair
. The
girl's brother
dives into the water to save her. Zatham tells the Shard-seeker to distract the beast while he would rescue the children. Unfortunately, the boy drowned before he could be saved.
After rescuing them, thay were attacked by cultists; which was a distraction for
their leader
to steal the
Worldstone
shard.

Last of the Horadrim
," he can be found at Backwater's docks, talking with
Teodar
,
Kiana
, and
Rodney
.
References

======================================================================
PAGE: Aodh Corraidhín
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Aodh_Corraidhín
======================================================================

Aodh Corraidhín
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Ethnicity
Glennfolk
Affiliation
Druids
Class
Druid
Relatives
Tadg (raven familiar)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Aodh Corraidhín
was a
druid
, and was once the guardian of the
Fréamh Loiscthe
. Though it was stolen under his watch, Aodh gave his life to prevent disaster.
Biography
Aodh was a master of shaping the
wind
, even amongst other druids.
At a point, he was given responsibility to guard the Fréamh Loiscthe, and ensure the
demon
within remains trapped.
To Aodh's great shame, the charred root was stolen by a
Vizjerei
infiltrator, a renegade to their own clan that dared invade
Túr Dúlra
under the guise of a rune crafter. Stoked by purpose and vengeance, Aodh summoned Tadg—his raven companion, and pursued the thief across northwestern
Scosglen
.
Aodh found the burnt remains of some of his coastal brethren, still hot and sizzling as the sea breeze steamed off their husks. With no druid to keep its burning fury contained, the demon within turned its ire back upon
Sanctuary
.
Aodh met with some
Ivgorodi
sailors about to return home. They were dismayed to hear of the slain coastal druids, and granted Aodh free passage across the sea to
the west
. His quarry had fled to
Ivgorod
, and they had to be warned of the danger in their midst.
The
Veradani
were wary at first of Aodh, but his descriptions of the Fréamh Loiscthe and the power it contained explained the recent "chaotic fire" they had witnessed in their lands. Worse still, a party of
khazra
had followed the infernal trail into
Gorgorra
Forest. A temporary accord was formed between monks and druid.
The alliance and the khazra caught up with the thief. The khazra were many, and the renegade Vizjerei had already begun a ritual to release the demon within the root, but the Veradani attacked them head-on. Aodh called upon the wolves of Gorgorra to harass the khazra as they withdrew with the wounded. The defeat was a great setback, for with the ritual underway, time was running out.
After sending Tadg to fly across the ritual site and coax the local animals away, Aodh stepped inside like the eye of a hurricane settling over a coastal gathering. The khazra howled as the wind pierced their eyes, and then screamed as the fires of the Fréamh Loiscthe were ignited and spread. The khazra burned, the Vizjerei burned... Aodh burned.
Legacy
Aodh had both stoked the fire within the charred root and protected the rest of Gorgorra from the flames. The surviving monks gave their blessings to
Ytar
and
Vaiyu
, along with thanks to the lost warrior from Scosglen for averting calamity. Tadg crowed a solemn song for his master before swooping down to clutch the Fréamh Loiscthe in his talons and begin the long flight home.
In-game
Aodh is mentioned in
Diablo Immortal
, in the flavor-text of the
Wildfire Imperative
item set
.

PAGE: Ashton Natoli

Ashton Natoli
Gender

Turn of a Card
Ashton Natoli
was the head of
House Natoli
.
Biography
Ashton married
Nerissa
. He got on well with her sister,
Elizabeth
, whom he recognised as a kindred spirit given their jovial approaches to life.
At some point after marrying, Ashton squandered Natoli's finances on gambling and booze. At some point he vanished, taking what little remained of the family fortune with him, leaving his wife to deal with the debts he had accumulated.
A year later, he turned up at the family manor, dead, left with nothing but the clothes he had on him. His body was taken around to the back courtyard. Perhaps not coincidentally, this was mere hours after Nerissa played a game with
Carlotta
, stating that what she desired most was for her husband to be returned to her. Certainly Nerissa suspected Carlotta of having a hand in her husband's murder.

======================================================================
PAGE: Atanna
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Atanna
======================================================================

"Atanna. A name that burried itself there and then in the veteran fighter's heart. Atanna, the most beautiful of beautiful women Captain Kentril Dumon had ever beheld. Atanna, an angel among mortals."
-
Kentril Dumon
's thoughts upon meeting Atanna
(
src
)
Atanna
Gender
Female
Race
Undead
human
Affiliation
Ureh
Relatives
Harkin Khan
(ancestor)
Zular Khan
(grandfather)
Juris Khan
(father)
Kentril Dumon
(consort)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
The Kingdom of Shadow
Atanna
was the daughter of
Juris Khan
, and an inhabitant of
Ureh
. She was well-versed in
magic
and music (specifically the flute), and was exceptionally beautiful.
Biography
The Fall of Ureh
"She was scared, my good captain, scared because she did not understand the gift he wished to give her. I had to be forceful. I had to
insist
...despite her unwillingness. It took much perseverance, even on the part of the archangel, but at last she opened up to him."
-
Juris Khan
on Atanna's corruption
(
src
)
Atanna lived in
Ureh
when the city was besieged by
Diablo
. In an effort to save themselves, her father and the city's
Sorcerers
attempted to cast a spell that would take the city into
Heaven
, under the guidance of the
Archangel
Mirakodus. However, Mirakodus was nothing but Diablo in disguise, and the spell would actually drag Ureh into
Hell
. The Sorcerer
Gregus Mazi
(whom Atanna may have been romantically entangled with) disrupted the spell, which left the city stuck in
Limbo
, and he himself cast out of the city.
Juris Khan, still in Diablo's thrall, and now ruler of a stranded city, followed the "archangel's" directions, and opened up his people to the "subtle ministrations of other angels." Or, in reality,
demons
. Atanna tried to resist, and gave Diablo himself pause, but he nonetheless forced himself into her. Like the rest of Ureh's people, Atanna became an
undead
monster.
The Return of Ureh
Thousands of years later, a band of mercenaries led by
Kentril Dumon
made their way into the city, having followed the guidance of the
Vizjerei
Sorcerer
Quov Tsin
. Her father introduced her to the mercenary captain. She served the mercenaries with food and drink as her father told them the (false) story of how Gregus Mazi had betrayed Ureh, stranding the city in Limbo and thwarting its people's attempt to ascend into
Heaven
, to escape from
Diablo
. She followed her father's line in describing Mazi. They told the Dumon how they might escape their fate if the
Key of Light
was placed atop
Mount Nymyr
; an impossible task for the people of Ureh, as they would burn if they stepped out of the city.
Dumon succeeded, and Ureh returned to the mortal realm, much to the joy of its citizenry, though a shadow needed to remain over the city, lest they burn from the sunlight. Dumon handed Atanna a brooch that contained her visage, one which he had found in the ruins of Ureh before he and the mercenaries had succeeded in entering it. She claimed that Mazi had desired her, and had stolen the brooch. She noticed Dumon clutch his
sword
, and asked if he would be her champion. Enraptured, Dumon declared that he would do anything for her, and she kissed him.
Dumon later encountered Atanna again in the palace, seeing her play the flute. She guided him through the gardens, and mended his hand after it was stung by something, presumably an insect (now possible as Ureh had returned to
Sanctuary
). In truth, no such sting had occurred, and Dumon had momentarily glimpsed Ureh's true, hellish state. Awhile later, she saw him again, thanking him in regards to Tsin, who had told her father that he might have found a way to completely solve Ureh's curse. He had likewise convinced her father that Ureh shouldn't try to ascend to Heaven again, that rather, ascending to Heaven would be something to be earned within the mortal realm. A celebratory dinner was held, with Dumon continuing to be enraptured by Atanna. He did, however, suffer a kind of panic attack (another glimpse of the nightmare that was Ureh), but Atanna got him to come to his senses.
Tsin's spell worked, and Dumon was made consort to Atanna. However, not all was well, and Dumon had come to suspect that something was wrong in Ureh, foremost of which was that a number of men had disappeared. She pouted, hoping that Dumon wasn't accusing her, but he pressed forward, telling her that her father hadn't slain Mazi, but had imprisoned him beneath the palace, turning him into some kind of hellish sentinel. Atanna momentarily lost her composure as Dumon continued to press that something was wrong, but regained it enough to try an alay his fears through seduction. She reached out for him, but something caused Dumon to surge forward, barging into Atanna and sending her plummeting off the palace balcony. The shadow made it too dark for him to see her body hit the ground, but there was no doubt in his mind that she should be dead.
And yet she wasn't, for she found Dumon with her father, desparately trying to explain that he hadn't meant to kill his daughter. One of her legs had snapped in the middle, her other foot was twisted on the side, her left arm was at an impossible angle, and her right was mangled beyond recognition. Physically, she was maimed, yet there was no sign of
blood
, and Atanna appeared to not even notice the damage that had been inflicted on her. Khan cast a spell and the damage appeared to heal, though her head still hung limply. Or at least it did, until Khan physically fixed it in place, as flesh and muscle fused, all sign of injury gone. Such was the power of Heaven, apparently, even while Dumon found the sight hellish. Atanna wasn't perturbed though...soon, she and Dumon would be together, and he'd be just like her. The true story of Ureh was soon revealed, and Atanna revealed herself as being so far gone, that she appeared enraptured at the memory of Diablo forcing himself onto her.
The time came to allow Ureh's people to enter Sanctuary proper. A ritual that would involve Dumon being a
blood
sacrifice. Atanna stroked her lover's hair, content that he would soon be like her, in an undead state. However, the ritual was interrupted by
one of Dumon's companions
, who absconded with the mercenary. Frustrated, Khan slew Tsin, completing the blood ritual, and thus, the stage was set for the people of Ureh to gain access to Sanctuary. All that remained was the sun to rise and touch the Key of Light atop Mount Nymyr. Atanna was assigned to guide the key, but was tormented as to what might happen to Dumon. Of what she might have to do to guard the key. She remembered the "archangel" that spoke to her, this time her memories tinged with both love and fear. She resolved that if Dumon confronted her, she would give him a test. Ideally, he would pass, but if not, he would die. She could accept that.
Dumon reached the key, but Atanna mentally contacted him, trying to sway his actions to not destroy it. Even her father attempted to keep the mercenary at bay, but he nonetheless threw the key off the top of the mountain. The sun rose, and Ureh's people burnt in its light. Dumon found himself falling down from the mountain, towards the city. About a hundred feet before the ground, however, Atanna, from the palace, used her magic to slow his fall. Even so far apart, their eyes locked, and her final moments, Atanna realized all she had done. Light began to shine over the palace, and she hastened the rate of his descent, but not so much that it would kill him. Yet the light reached her, and as it rose up her body, Atanna simply faded away.
Her actions weren't in vain however, and while injured, Dumon survived the fall. Two days later, he departed the ruins of Ureh with his surviving fellows, yet still kept the brooch that held Atanna's image.

PAGE: Bay
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Bay
======================================================================

Bay
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Occupation
Farmer (formerly)
Relatives
Parents, deceased
Status
Likely deceased
Appearances
Tales of Sanctuary
Bay
was a young farm girl, taken as a sacrifice by the
Zakarum
.
Biography
Bay lived on a farm with her father and mother. Their farm was situated close to a Zakarum cathedral, and many times the priests would come to the farm, demanding tithes for their holy works. Every time her father would refuse, as he was not a follower of the Zakarum faith. On what would be the priests' last visit, an argument broke out, the priests declaring that he would regret his defiance.
Not long after that, the farm came under attack by
khazra
. In the past, Bay and her family would always hide whenever they passed by, and the creatures did not seem to notice them. This time however, they did. The creatures attacked, setting the farm alight, killing Bay's mother. Her father tried to ward the creatures off with a pitchfork, but he was killed in turn. Bay was saved however, by a
Paladin
named
Hale
, who slew the creatures. He buried her parents, and offered to give her sanctuary in the Zakarum. Bay took him to the Zakarum cathedral, wondering if her father had listened to the priests, perhaps he'd still be alive.
Bay is taken away by the curate
Arriving at the cathedral, they were granted entry. Bay was frightened by the cathedral's grim interior, and the wall carvings that depicted all manner of
demons
. Hale explained that it was a representation of the evil the Zakarum combatted, an assertion repeated by the cathedral's
curate
. He declared that he would take Bay into the church, and teach her in the ways of the Zakarum. Hale departed to his assigned quarters, while Bay was taken to the depths of the cathedral to be sacrificed. She called out for Hale, and he burst into the chamber before the ritual could be completed. The curate revealed that they, and Zakarum as a whole, were in service to
Mephisto
, and Bay would be sacrificed to him. Hale cut his way through the priests, but couldn't reach Bay and the curate in time. He
teleported
away with Bay, declaring that Bay's
blood
would please the Lord of Hatred.
References

======================================================================
PAGE: Big Adhelm
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Big_Adhelm
======================================================================

Big Adhelm
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Olaud's Hutches
Relatives
Brother Adhelm
,
Little Adhelm
(brothers),
Lady Adhelm
(sister)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Big Adhelm
was a member of the Adhelm line, and resident of
Olaud's Hutches
.
Biography
The Adhelms stole wool and fur from the dead in Olaud's Hutches, and was cast free to wander, with no provisions and nothing but the clothes on their backs, to expire or to prove their fellow-feeling.
From the first, the wanderers' hunts were meager, and their shivering slowed their limbs and scared the game away. They blamed Lady Adhelm for resting while the others tried and failed. But Lady Adhelm knew that to hunt in weakness was futile, and a single rabbit was not near enough to feed the four of them. She conserved her strength.
At their failure and the Lady's sloth, the wanderers' blood ran hot, and they fell to anger amongst themselves. They shouted and raved, but did not strike with the axes and clubs they had fashioned, and instead marched on, for shedding the
blood
of their kin would mean they would be forever forbidden in the Hutches.
The wanderers came upon a lake, but it was frozen solid, and they could not see the fish below. Their bellies grumbled in unison, and as they stood to leave,
Little Adhelm
did not rise. Lady Adhelm lay Little Adhelm in downy snow, where no trees cast their shadow, and marked him by a cairn of gray stones, and the wanderers vowed to look nevermore upon his body at her behest.
The three remaining Adhelms walked until the glory of an icewall rose before them, and they could travel no further. Big Adhelm sunk down in despair, and Lady Adhelm and her
brother
prayed over him, and Lady Adhelm carved signs of him into the ice. But he did not rise, and they turned, and did not stop their wandering.
Big Adhelm's flesh was later consumed by his sister
before she returned to Olaud's Hutches.

PAGE: Boyce
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Boyce
======================================================================

"Toughen up, little sprite. Indulge the instincts. This will go quick."
- Boyce to
Alodie
(
src
)
Boyce
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Occupation
Criminal, enforcer
Relatives
Mother
Various siblings
Alodie
(cousin)
Status
Active
Appearances
Instincts
Boyce
was the son of a criminal matriarch in
Kingsport
.
Boyce was gaunt. He was "deeper in the
blood
" with "a nose so proud it served as his face from most angles."
Alodie
considered him to be a boor.
Biography
Boyce's role was a "settler," specifically an individual who followed up on those who had fallen into debt with the family. The family had an arrangement with a
vampire
that stalked the
Solterwood
north of Kingsport. The family would provide it individuals who had fallen into debt, and the vampire would turn them into
thralls
. The vampire in question appeared to be a familial ancestor. When she learnt about the arrangement, Alodie speculated that the family's motivations for serving the vampire was for either money, protection, or some form of
bloodline
obligation.
Alodie was Boyce's cousin, and she worked with him as a "settler." She generally played the role of peacemaker, while Boyce was the muscle.
Instincts
"You really don’t have the instincts. I think, if she’s going to take our livelihood, we should take hers. That makes sense."
- Boyce before breaking
Linn
's knuckles
(
src
)
In what would be their last job together, Boyce and Alodie visited
Linn
, who had fallen into debt with the family. Boyce smashed various glasses and stuffed a rag in Linn's mouse before grabbing a hammer, intent on shattering her teeth. As usual, Alodie tried to play peacemaker, much to Boyce's disappointment. Instead of breaking her teeth, Boyce broke the knuckles of Linn's right hand, despite Alodie pointing out that this would prevent her from repaying the family, as she needed her hands for her livelihood. He nonchelantly said that there was a way Linn could pay them back without a few weeks' work.
Boyce took Linn and bound her in a carriage, adding her to the bodies of various individuals that had fallen into debt with the family. Individuals that would be offered to the vampire. Boyce and his crew headed into the Solterwood with their
human
cargo. They exchanged the delivery with their fellow gang members, who took them deeper into the wood.

PAGE: Brother Adhelm
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Brother_Adhelm
======================================================================

Brother Adhelm
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Olaud's Hutches
Relatives
Big Adhelm
,
Little Adhelm
(brothers),
Lady Adhelm
(sister)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Brother Adhelm
was a member of the Adhelm line, and resident of
Olaud's Hutches
.
Biography
The Adhelms stole wool and fur from the dead in Olaud's Hutches, and was cast free to wander, with no provisions and nothing but the clothes on their backs, to expire or to prove their fellow-feeling.
From the first, the wanderers' hunts were meager, and their shivering slowed their limbs and scared the game away. They blamed Lady Adhelm for resting while the others tried and failed. But Lady Adhelm knew that to hunt in weakness was futile, and a single rabbit was not near enough to feed the four of them. She conserved her strength.
At their failure and the Lady's sloth, the wanderers' blood ran hot, and they fell to anger amongst themselves. They shouted and raved, but did not strike with the axes and clubs they had fashioned, and instead marched on, for shedding the
blood
of their kin would mean they would be forever forbidden in the Hutches.
The wanderers came upon a lake, but it was frozen solid, and they could not see the fish below. Their bellies grumbled in unison, and as they stood to leave,
Little Adhelm
did not rise. Lady Adhelm lay Little Adhelm in downy snow, where no trees cast their shadow, and marked him by a cairn of gray stones, and the wanderers vowed to look nevermore upon his body at her behest.
The three remaining Adhelms walked until the glory of an icewall rose before them, and they could travel no further. Big Adhelm sunk down in despair, and Lady Adhelm and Brother Adhelm prayed over him, and Lady Adhelm carved signs of him into the ice. But he did not rise, and they turned, and did not stop their wandering.
Now, only Lady and Brother Adhelm remained. They walked, and Brother Adhelm faltered. Brother Adhelm asked his sister why she was still strong, and she replied that her faith kept her strong. At this Brother Adhelm yearned for his faith, and put his head upon the snow to rest, and Lady Adhelm said she would go to seek warmth and food for him, and vanished into the falling sleet.
Brother Adhelm presumably froze to death, as Lady Adhelm returned to Olaud's Hutches as the sole survivor of the Adhelms.

======================================================================
PAGE: Buyard Cholik
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Buyard_Cholik
======================================================================

Buyard Cholik
was a former Zakarum priest who brought back the demon Kabraxis. He is one of the main characters of
The Black Road
novel.
Background
Buyard Cholik had been a loyal acolyte of the Zakarum-priesthood for most of his life. As the Zakarum religion slowly fell under
Mephisto
's malevolent sway, Cholik became intrigued by the dark forces in control of Zakarum. As Cholik aged, he became increasingly fearful of death and frustrated with the - in his eyes - insignificant powers of the Light. Therefore he turned his back on the Zakarum religion, and started researching more sinister powers. Through long forgotten texts Cholik learned about the demon
Kabraxis
, who was supposedly powerful enough to grant mortals eternal life. Desperate to extend his life and hungry for power, Cholik started to search for Kabraxis' prison.
With the aid of the demon he created a new religion ; the Way of Dreams ; where the followers worshiped the demon himself. During this era he was known as the Wayfinder ; the right hand of the prophet Dien-Ap-Sten (Kabraxis). He was later kiled by Darrick Lang who wielded Stormfury ; an old holy sword that was the only weapon that could defeat Kabraxis.
This article is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Cadeus
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Cadeus
======================================================================

Caedus
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Class
Healer
Occupation
Healer
Status
Active
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
Cadeus
is a healer based on
Bilefen
.
He has a
hut
in the
Northern Wetlands
.
Biography
Among the Bodies
In
1270
, Cadeus was approached by
the Shard-seeker
, sent to find him by
Talva Silvertongue
. They spoke of a nearby
village
, and that Talva believed it to be cursed. Cadeus scoffed at such a suggestion, instead stating that a creature was behind the village's suffering. If they killed the creature, the suffering would end.
The group came to a river where they found a
corpse
floating in it, having come downriver. Cadeus pointed out that it wasn't
magic
that was behind this, but rather, that the body had been injected with a toxin. He advised the hero(es) to head upriver and follow the bodies. By doing so, they could discover what was behind this.
Cadeus arrives in the village
Cadeus later found the hero(es) in the village by the remains of
Elder Owen
. As it had turned out, a
Maggot Brood
had poisoned the village, killing all its inhabitants bar Owen. While
Corpse Worms
had writhed inside him, a beacon taken from the
Temple of Namari
had kept him alive, even as the worms consumed him from the inside. Cadeus lamented Owen's fate, but the hero(es) pointed out that there was another beacon on the island, and it could be causing even more damage. Cadeus directed them to
Rikari Village
, believing that it was in the hands of the
Fetishes
.
Cadeus felt somewhat guilty for not being able to save Owens, so he started researching means of making an antidote to the
plague
. He was able to make a prototype. Later, there was a resurgence of the plague in
Port Justinian
, and even Cadeus was infected. He enlisted the help of an adventurer to get a sample of infected water, so that he may perfect his antidote. By adulterating the new antidote with the original prototype he was able to make a cure for the green death.
Bounties
Note: The following events aren't necessarily linked in chronological order.
Caedus requested that
adventurers
clear out the
Northern Wetlands
of
Ichthids
, as the herbs he needed for his medicines grew best there.
He similarly requested adventurers to gather
Toxic Lurker
venom from
spiders
in the
Dark Wood
, so he could use it as an anesthetic.
As he continued to study the Bilefen plague, he requested that
Plague Stinger
specimens be delivered to him.
In-game
Cadeus is an
NPC
in
Diablo Immortal
. He is found in the
Northern Wetlands
during the "
Among the Bodies
"
quest
.
He provides the "
It's Always Ichthids
," "
Plague Research
," and "
Numbing the Pain
"
bounties
.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
As a healer, Cadeus is possibly named in reference to the
Caduceus
; a symbol sometimes used in medicine.
Cadeus is among those who knows at least some of the true nature of the
Temple of Namari
; he is aware that it was designed not as a temple, but as a prison, for "
something
."

PAGE: Captain Haile
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Captain_Haile
======================================================================

"That was Captain Haile of
Westmarch
. He’s won hundreds of lost causes all over the
world
. I heard the
king
had to threaten him with treason just to get him to return home for a promotion."
-
Kormac
(
src
)
Hansen Haile
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Westmarch
Occupation
Captain
Status
Kyla Haile
(daughter)
Appearances
Diablo III
Diablo III: Reaper of Souls
Captain
Hansen Haile
is a soldier of
Westmarch
.
Biography
Haile served Westmarch and won great fame for himself. He "won hundreds of lost causes" all over
Sanctuary
. Supposedly, King
Justinian IV
had to threaten him with treason just to get him to return home to accept a promotion.
The Siege of Bastion's Keep
""More of the brutes from below, Captain! What do we do?"
"Private, if you need to be told which end of the
sword
goes where, you haven’t been paying attention! Fight to your last breath, lads!"
- Hansen rallies his men
(
src
)
In
1285
, Haile, now a captain, was stationed at
Bastion's Keep
when it was
besieged
by
Azmodan
. He led his men at the
Stonefort
.
During the siege, a
Siegebreaker Assault Beast
was unleashed upon the fortress, though Haile and 100 soldiers were able to bring it down.
On the ninth day of the siege, Commander
Calderos
planned to lead a charge out of the keep on the following day, intending to scatter the demons. Haile commented that Calderos could "commit suicide by stupidity" if he wanted to, but he'd be damned if he sent any of his men with him.
By the time
The Nephalem
arrived, Haile was down to just four soldiers. With The Nephalem's aid, his men was able to raise one of the catapults, holding the
demons
at bay. Haile told The Nephalem that it was an honor to fight at their side.
Haile encountered The Nephalem again later in the battle at
Rakkis Crossing
; all of his men had perished during the charge against Azmodan's lair. The Nephalem aided him in fighting off a group of demons.
Azmodan
was defeated, but
Adria
betrayed her allies, killing numerous people in the keep, and allowing
Diablo
to be reborn. Haile survived, but fell into despair, suffering from survivor's guilt, and asking what the point of it all was—to hold off Azmodan long enough for Diablo to return? The Nephalem pointed out that there were still those who relied on him, but he bitterly pointed out that his men had as well, and they were now dead.
The Nephalem travelled to Heaven and returned to Bastion's Keep as necessary. Haile reacted in awe that The Nephalem was still alive. Inspired by their actions, he resolved to do what he could to keep up spirits within the fortress.
Towards the end of the battle, Haile asked them to think of his lads when they struck
Diablo
down.
The Fall of Westmarch
This section is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
While exploring
Briarthorn cemetery
you may encounter Haile with several soldiers, he greets you as a friend before a horde of
reapers
attack in 3 waves ending with
Ankou
. After their death you are rewarded some gold and exp.
In-game
Haile is encountered in
Act III
of
Diablo III
. He is first encountered as an
NPC
in the
quest
"
Turning the Tide
," where the player fights off
monsters
while his men raise a catapult. In
Act IV
, he is an NPC in the
Bastion's Keep Stronghold
hub area.
In
Act V
, the player enters Captain Haile's home and rescues his daughter
Kyla
and her friend (a small boy from Bastion's Keep) and helps them escape to the
Survivor's Enclave
. The player can later find Haile himself in Westmarch, where he helps slaughter a large group of reapers before departing. Captain Haile appears again later on, reunited with his daughter. He happily informs Kyla and her friend that the Reapers have finally been cleared out of Westmarch and soon will be defeated completely.

PAGE: Captain Rumford
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Captain_Rumford
======================================================================

"The tireless farmer Rumford is one of the many respectable individuals I have met in
New Tristram
. He seems a humble and introverted man, but I think there is more to him than that. I have heard that his ancestor was one of
Rakkis
's most loyal lieutenants, a charismatic soldier who settled in
Khanduras
. Due to this lineage, I believe the
blood
of a leader runs through Rumford's veins, whether he knows it or not."
-
Deckard Cain
(
src
)
Rumford
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Tristram Militia
Occupation
Farmer
Militia captain
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo III
Book of Tyrael
(mentioned only)
Rumford
was a member of a
Tristram Militia
. While humble and introverted, he proved himself to be a capable leader when
New Tristram
was assailed by the
undead
.
Biography
Rumford's ancestry goes back to the
Sons of Rakkis
. His ancestor was one of
Rakkis
's most loyal lieutenants. The soldier came to settle in
Khanduras
.
Rumford himself lived in/near
New Tristram
.
His grandfather told him stories of ancient heroes who performed impossible feats, but also told his grandson that he looked like a
Quill Fiend
. He was, in Rumford's words, "a strange man."
In Khanduras, Rumford worked as a farmer, and also served as a member of the
Tristram Militia
. In
1284
, he met
Deckard Cain
, who had arrived in the village alongside his adopted niece,
Leah
. He made a good impression on Cain.
The Fallen Star
"I volunteered to help because it seemed the right thing to do. But I’m no leader of men."
"True, though you have held the town thus far."
"That’s a simple thing for you to say. You were born to fight monsters like the risen dead. Me, I’m just a farmer."
- Rumford and
The Nephalem
(
src
)
The
following year
, a
fallen star
descended from the
Heavens
above New Tristram, causing the
dead
to rise from their slumber. When Leah emerged from the ruins of the
Tristram Cathedral
, she told the militia that undead were pouring out of the cathedral. Rumford and fifteen other militia marched upon the cathedral under the command of
Captain Daltyn
, and while they did well at first, the dead just kept coming. Only Rumford survived, and he returned to New Tristram, now the captain of the miltia.
Rumford meets with The Nephalem
Rumford and the remaining militia held the gates of New Tristram against the undead
for six days. Morale sagged.
The situation improved when they were aided by
The Nephalem
, who was able to make short work of the creatures. Rumford told them that if they wanted to learn about the fallen star, they should talk to Leah. As The Nephalem entered the town, he ordered the guards to burn the bodies, lest they rise again.
The Nephalem returned, and told Rumford that they intended to put an end to the
Risen Dead
. He told them to strike at the
Wretched Mothers
. When The Nephalem returned to New Tristram, victorious, Rumford told them to talk to Leah. She hadn't given up hope of finding her uncle, and he wanted the hero to talk some sense into her.
In truth, Leah set out with The Nephalem to rescue Cain. With The Nephalem gone, the militia were left to defend the town. Rumford reduced the rations to halves and quarters.

stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
In-game
Captain Rumford
Appears in
Diablo III
Service(s)
Gossip, Quest initiation

New Tristram
Starts quest(s)

Captain Rumford appears as an

in

of

. He plays a role in "

" quest.
At the start of the quest "
Trailing the Coven
," he will no longer be found in the center of town. Upon leaving
New Tristram
and heading towards the
Old Ruins
, he can be found lying dead at the bridge.
His ghost/
soul
has a chance to appear in
Act IV
, but upon interaction, he will accuse
the Nephalem
of letting greed drive their actions, and failing to save him. After that, he turns into the monster
Aspect of Sin
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Celia
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Celia
======================================================================

The following article contains information from  the
Diablo I
expansion
Hellfire
, which is of ambiguous canon status.
"I lost Theo! I lost my best friend! We were playing over by the river, and Theo said he wanted to go look at the big green thing. I said we shouldn't, but we snuck over there, and the suddenly this bug came out! We ran away but Theo fell down and the bug grabbed him and took him away!"
- Celia
(
src
)
Celia
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Affiliation
Khanduras
Appearances
Diablo: Hellfire
Celia
was an inhabitant of
Tristram
.
Biography
Celia held great attachment to a teddy bear named Theodore ("Theo" for short). During the
Darkening of Tristram
, she and Theo were playing by the
River Talsande
. Theo 'told' her that he wanted to look at the "big green thing." Celia didn't, but they went over anyway. Suddenly, a large insect came out. Celia ran away, but Theo fell (a.k.a. was dropped), and the insect took him into the depths of the
Festering Nest
.
Celia found some help at the hands of a
hero
, who entered the Nest, slew the
Hork Demon
, and returned Theo to Celia. Celia went home with her teddy after thanking the "hero person" who helped her.
In-game
Celia is exclusive to
Diablo: Hellfire
. She initiates the
Little Girl
quest. However, she was cut from the final release of the expansion, and can only be seen if the player uses the
Command.txt exploit
. She appears on
Adria's
island, near the bridge, but not until the player has entered the Festering Nest.
She is one of the few
NPCs
who changes appearance in the game. After the player retrieves Theo for her she can be seen holding him in her arms. If the Hork Demon drops a random amulet instead of Theo if slain, an equivalent amulet will be given by Celia upon returning Theo to her. Interestingly, Celia speaks of Theodore as of a living being (which is understandable for a little girl), and until the moment of slaying the Hork Demon, players will not find out that Theo is actually a toy.

======================================================================
PAGE: Chancellor Eamon
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Chancellor_Eamon
======================================================================

Eamon
Title
Chancellor Eamon
Astral Guardian
Gender
Male
Race
(
Undead
)
human
Affiliation
Khanduras
Class
Wraith
Occupation
Chancellor
Relatives
Haedrig Eamon
(grandson)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo III
Chancellor Eamon, Astral Guardian,
is a
Super Unique
Wraith
in
Diablo III
. He is the spirit of
Haedrig Eamon
's grandfather,
Biography
Before heading for
Khanduras
, Eamon had a son, who in turn had a
son of his own
. They were living in
Caldeum
when Eamon left with
Leoric
and his forces to journey to
Khanduras
, where Leoric set up his seat of power in
Tristram
. During the
Darkening of Tristram
, Eamon remained in the town, trying to save lives.
As Leoric descended further into madness, he ordered Eamon to seal the
caves
near his
manor
, in order to protect his estate from the "traitorous rabble" in Tristram. He informed him that
Archbishop Lazarus
had bound some
spiders
to his will,
and ordered the caverns filled with them. Eamon was unable to get the king to change his mind, and sorrowfully ordered the Royal Guard to obey the king's command, desecrating the ruins within the caverns.
When Leoric was killed by his
knights
, Eamon was dying from a
sword
wound. He was buried in a
tomb
and had
Leoric's Crown
sealed with him.
Over
twenty years later
, Eamon was resurrected (likely as a result of the
Fallen Star
. He was confronted by
The Nephalem
, who sought Leoric's crown. Eamon tried to prevent them from claiming it, but failed, dying a second time. The crown was broken, and The Nephalem wondered if Eamon had done this himself, to prevent anyone from abusing it. Neverthless, the crown was reforged.
In-game
Chancellor Eamon
Eamon is found in the
Chancellor's Tomb
in
Act I
of
Diablo III
. He protects Leoric's Crown, an item the player has to recover in order to defeat the
Skeleton King
during the quest "
A Shattered Crown
." The crown may not be taken until Chancellor Eamon is defeated.
His attack has a very potent Slow on every hit. In addition, he has Knockback and Teleporter affixes.
Quotes
"No! I will not allow you to bring that monster Leoric back to this world!"

Biography
Note: The following events aren't necessarily in chronological order.
Kaya beholds Skarn
Kaya led the Westmarch Guard in the defense of the
capital
when it was attacked by

's

. She fought alongside

Sanctuary
until
humanity
begged for his salvation. Kaya ordered the Shard-seeker to hunt down Skarn's forces, and declared that if Skarn desired hell, Westmarch would give it to him.
In a future foreseen by the
Einfrinn Tree

Lassal the Flame-spun
when the
Wrathborne
invaded Westmarch.
However, this future was apparently avoided.
Kaya used her rank to allow the Shard-seeker investigate the
red boulder
that crashed beyond
the Wolf Gate
.
Later, the Shard-seeker reported an averted attack on the
Black Bower
by sea monsters. Kaya decided to double the patrol at
the Docks
, and advised them to be quiet about it, as the city doesn't like a panic.

Corik Trost
Title
The Abandoned
Gender
Male
Race
(
Undead
)
human
Relatives
Vendral Trost
(father)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo IV
Corik Trost, The Abandoned
is a
monster
in
Diablo IV
.
Biography
Corik was the son of
Vendral Trost
. During the
Great Enmity
, he was imprisoned in the
Black Asylum
for supposedly murdering a boy his age. Whether this actually occurred however, is debatable—Corik later claimed that his father lied, that he had never had the courage to face him. Vendral himself later commented that Corik had been sent away "for a sin of my own making," and that the
blood
was on his own hands.
Whatever the truth of Corik's innocence (or lack of it), he was left in the Black Asylum with numerous other inmates when it was abandoned and apparently sealed. The lucky ones were said to have starved, while the rest escaped their cells only to fight each other. Like so many others, Corik's
spirit
lingered in the asylum's walls, unable to move on.
In
1336
, Corik's spirit was haunting his father, appearing as he had as a young boy rather than the young man he had grown up to be in the asylum.
The Wanderer
obliged Vendral in entering the asylum and laying Corik's spirit to rest, but noted that Corik had loathed his father to the end. Vendral claimed to still hear Corik's voice, and wandered off into the snow, telling his son that he was coming.
In-game
Corik's younger form
Corik is encountered in the
side quest
"
Cries of Innocence
." He is found in the first area of the Black Asylum. He attacks via melee. He appears as a faint apparition at the start of the quest as well, much younger, apparently indicating the amount of time between his imprisonment and death.

Coshumat
was a count who lived in the late 10th/early 11th centuries. He ruled over starving fiefs, yet refused bread and succor to those who did not impress him. All that

PAGE: Covetous Shen

======================================================================

"I'm a simple man. Give me a good meal, a warm bed, and a handful of jewels."
- Covetous Shen
(src)
Covetous Shen
Title
The Jeweler
Gender
Male
Affiliation
Xiansai
(formerly)
Artisans
The Nephalem
Class
Jeweler
Relatives
Myriam Jahzia
(former wife)
Various other former wives (well over seven)
Status
Unknown
