Gossip about Greiz
Some of the other locals give their thoughts concerning Greiz.
Elzix
I miss the brothels that used to do business here. You know, all of the ladies fled to the palace as soon as the trouble in the desert started. You'd think that they could at least come out once in a while now that Greiz and his men have things relatively under control.
Fara
Greiz is a fine warrior and leader, but in his heart, he will always be a mercenary for hire. I cannot be loyal to those who have no loyalty to themselves.
Geglash
Greiz seems to have this place locked down nice and tight. Not that I couldn't have done the same! I've proven my valor in combat plenty of times.
Jerhyn
Greiz, the mercenary captain I hired to secure the gates of Lut Gholein, keeps order in town, as well.
Lysander
Oh... I have great faith in Greiz. He seems to have things well in hand.
Meshif
Greiz seems to be a dependable fellow. I hope he can handle it if those things in the desert decide to attack this town.

Greta
is an
NPC
in
Westmarch
in
Diablo Immortal
. She can be found in

, looking for her kitten.
C.

Hadeen
was an inhabitant of
Toraja
during the early years of
Sanctuary
. Unlike many of his fellow Torajans, Hadeen did not follow
Uldyssian
in his quest to undo both the
Triune
and the
Cathedral of Light
.
After the destruction of the Triune temple at Toraja (which left parts of the city in ruin) the cunning angel
Inarius
sent emissaries to Toraja, convincing the townsfolk that the
Edyrem
were bent on destroying all of
Kehjan
. Hadeen joined the makeshift peasant army and attacked the Edyrem, resulting in their deaths.

======================================================================
PAGE: Halissa
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Halissa
======================================================================

Halissa
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Affiliation
Westmarch
(formerly, presumed)
Relatives
Valla
(sister)
Unnamed sawyer (parent)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
Diablo III
(mentioned only)
Diablo III: Reaper of Souls
(player determinant)
Hatred and Discipline
(mentioned only)
Halissa
was the sister of
Valla
.
Biography
Life
The daughter of a sawyer,
Halissa and her family resided in
Westmarch
,
in
a village
close to
Tristram
, located in a forest.
She was close to Valla, and her face always lit up at the sight of her.
Halissa's family were killed by
demons
, when the Hellspawn attacked their village. Valla grabbed Halissa and they ran to the river and hid for weeks. Memories of the massacre gave her nightmares and "unhinged" her mind. One stormy
night she woke up screaming and ran, coming too close to the riverbank and slipping
. Valla, who had chased after her, tried to grab her hand, but lost her grip and she was swept away in the current,
raving and cursing
before drowning.
Her
soul
wound up in the
Pandemonium Fortress
. She looked for her parents, but couldn't find them. But she knew they were somewhere nearby. She could hear them screaming.
Death
Valla at her family's graves
Valla erected a gravestone for Halissa beside the graves of her parents. She later joined the
Demon Hunters
, and kept an etching of her sister on hand, even two decades after her death. Halissa's death continued to haunt her, and the memories were used against her by the demon
Valdraxxis
. Just prior to her departure for
Khanduras
in light of premonitions of a
Fallen Star
, she visited Halissa's grave again.
Years after her death,
Malthael
led the
Reapers
against
Sanctuary
.
Ordan
instructed
Halissa
in the means to communicate with the living. Sure enough, Valla encountered Halissa within the Pandemonium Fortress. As Halissa explained, "something bad" kept her soul in the fortress, and asked Valla to remove it.
This section is a
stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by
expanding it
.
In-game
In
Diablo III
, Halissa appears within the Pandemonium Fortress in
Act V
, provided the player is controlling a Demon Hunter. The game operates under the premise of her being the sibling of the Demon Hunter, regardless of the character's gender (the same principle applies to the Demon Hunter's cinematic intro and journal entries). She is depicted as a little girl armed with a
Hand Crossbow
.
Halissa's "older" portrait
Her initial portrait found in the game files shows her as a young woman (not a girl) with similar facial features.
Personality and Traits
Valla described Halissa as possessing bright, inquisitive eyes, and boundless energy.

Hamit
was an undercover Terror Cultist.
Biography
Hamit, along with
Iockin
were sent by the
Cult of Terror
to
Westmarch
in an undercover mission to gather resources and research on a way to send the
Worldstone
shard to
Diablo
. While in Westmarch, they stayed in the
Wolf City Tavern
. They also rented a

in the
Storehouse District
where they did their research and conducted sacrifices.
Unfortunately, their excessive swagger attracted the attention of spies;
one
of which was paid by
Zatham
to look for suspicious behavior. Zatham bid
the Shard-seeker
to investigate, who was able to follow them back to their hideaway. He was later killed along with Iockin by the Shard-seeker.
In-game
Hamit and Iockin are fought in the Cultists Dwelling after the player trails them there. He has the abilities of a standard Deadwright. Though he has a unique name, he is not an
elite monster
.

Hanso
was a ship captain.
At some point after the
Mage Clan Wars
, he captained a ship from
Kingsport
which sailed north-east on a mining expedition. His first mate,
McMahon
, became seasick, but while Hanso offered him ale to alleviate his symptoms, McMahon refused each time.
During their trip, the ship ran into a storm, and after being battered for three days, a tidal wave carried them inland to
Kehjistan
. Hanso disappeared in the desert shortly afterwards.

PAGE: Holus
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Holus
======================================================================

"Your cart is in the way."
"How dare you speak to me like that! I am the mayor of this town!"
"Then why are you standing here, idle?"
"Are you mad? This town is doomed! Anyone with a grain of sense should be trying to get out! Will you help me or not?"
"No."
-
The Nephalem
and Holus
(
src
)
Holus
Title
Mayor Holus
Former Mayor Holus
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
New Tristram
(formerly)
Occupation
Mayor of New Tristram (formerly)
Merchant
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo III
Storm of Light
(mentioned only)
The Art of Diablo III
The Art of Diablo
Holus
was the mayor of
New Tristram
. During the
End of Days
, he met his end at
Bastion's Keep
.
Biography
Once a merchant
who came to
New Tristram
, Holus became mayor of the town soon after. While he was an adequate ruler of the town in times of peace, his bravery proved to be quite lacking when the
Fallen Star
hit the old
cathedral
and the
dead
began to rise to attack the town.
The Mayor, fearing for his life, tried to flee the town and take his broken cart with him, regardless of the blockage it caused. He claimed that the town was doomed and that anyone with a grain of sense would flee. His cowardice disgusted both the townsfolk and
The Nephalem
, who refused to help him. Eventually, the townsfolk dragged his cart aside, leaving him to wallow in his despair
before fleeing.
Making his living as a merchant once again, Holus made his way to Bastion's Keep, only to find the fortress under siege by
Azmodan
's
demons
. Here, he encountered The Nephalem again. Certain that if he stayed he would be slaughtered, he offered to pay the Nephalem anything if it would gain him an escort to safety. The Nephalem refused,
and continued to do so as the siege progressed. Eventually, Holus rationalized that it was perhaps safer to stay and, if it came to it, fight. The Nephalem was taken by surprise by his change in attitude, surprised again when it was discovered that Holus had indeed stayed. As Holus stated, while he wasn't brave, he wasn't a liar.
Holus's body
The siege was thrown back and the demons defeated.
However,
Adria
turned on the keep's defenders, killing many of them. Holus stood his ground and fought, a defiance which cost him his life.
In-game
Mayor Holus/Former Mayor Holus
Appears in
Diablo III
Significance
Moderate
Service(s)
Mayor
Residence(s)
New Tristram
Bastion's Keep
Holus is encountered as an
NPC
throughout
Diablo III
.
In
Act I
, Holus is designated as "Mayor Holus," and can be found blocking the way into the rest of the town with his personal belongings in a cart. After the player visits the
Cathedral
for the first time, his cart will be removed from the road, permitting the player to explore the rest of the town.
Upon arriving in
Act III
, he can be found inside of
Bastion's Keep
once again cowering for his life. His name also slightly changes, gaining the title of "Former Mayor." Through the act, he will often give foresight into the oncoming quest, and the hero will encourage him to be a braver man.
Immediately after beginning
Act IV
, if the player returns to Bastion's Keep, they can find his corpse in his previous location. A nearby guard will explain how he stood his ground till the very end.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
During development, Holus's name was "Fennan."

======================================================================
PAGE: Hungering Moon
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Hungering_Moon
======================================================================

"The
moon
is hungry, and it demands
blood
...perhaps even yours! You,
adventurer
, gaze upon the moon—bask in its hallowed glow, heed its howl for sustenance, and lunar-laced blessings you shall be bestowed. Fulfilling the moon's demands will earn you
Moonslivers
, which can be traded for Blessings. After acquiring seven Blessings you will have curried enough goodwill with the moon to trade these in for a random reward. Offer enough blessings to the moon and it will even present you with its favor."
- Character description
(src)
Hungering Moon
Gender
Male
Status
Active
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
The
Hungering Moon
is an
NPC
(of sorts) in
Diablo Immortal
.
The Moon is a generous entity, and rewards its most faithful followers handsomely.
Gameplay
The Hungering Moon was first introduced in
Season
2 of
Diablo Immortal
, and has returned on a regular basis. During the periods where the Moon is active, players can acquire
moonslivers
and trade them in for blessings. Every seven blessings can be traded in for a random reward. The Moon interface can be accessed through the "Events" tab of the game's menu.
The event runs from 3 a.m. on a Saturday until 3 a.m. on the next Friday. Players can complete up to three tasks a day four times. Through completing tasks, they'll gain Astrolabe Power—the power can be used to draw one of two types of blessings with unique benefits from the Astrolabe.
The blessings are as follows, with the moonsliver rewards:
Blessing of More:
+50% experience while in dungeons for 10 minutes - 5
+20% critical hit chance while in dungeons for 10 minutes - 5
Blessing of Might: Complete any X dungeon solo or in a party to earn
1 dungeon - 10+10
2 dungeons - 20+20
3 dungeons - 30+30
If the dungeon is completed in a party first, the solo reward is also awarded. For the purposes of Hungering Moon, completing a dungeon with
Spectral Allies
counts as completing it in a party.
The Hermit's Collection (located within the Hungering Moon event tab) can be accessed to trade moonslivers for lunar-laced rewards. Collecting and using 12 blessings in total earns The Moon's Regard—a bounty of 90 bonus moonslivers.
The Hungering Moon will reward players with the following materials if they collect the listed amount of moonslivers during the event's duration. No moonslivers need to be spent to acquire the materials:
10 Moonslivers: 3
Rare Crests
50 Moonslivers: 1 random
Set Item
130 Moonslivers: 1
Telluric Pearl
230 Moonslivers: 1
Legendary Crest
Moonslivers can be spent on the following rewards:
Normal Gem
- 15  (max: 4)
Mystery
Legendary Item
65 (max: 65)
Aspirant's Key
- 4 (max: 15)
Reinforced Scrap Materials
- 10 (max: 7)
Flowing Shard
- 15 (max: 3)
1000 Gold - 1 (max: 60)
Completing all the tasks (including taking the Moon's Regard) rewards exactly enough moonslivers to buy all the rewards.
History
While
Event Center
was active (first run between May 4 and 11, 2024), Seal of Triumph rewards were added to the milestone rewards:
10 Moonslivers: 4
Seal of Triumph
50 Moonslivers: 7
Seal of Triumph
130 Moonslivers: 11
Seal of Triumph
230 Moonslivers: 22
Seal of Triumph
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
Taking the character blurb as being literal, the Hungering Moon seems to be
the
moon
of
Sanctuary
, personified. However, there is no in-game lore associated with the Hungering Moon.

======================================================================

is a
Shardborne
, and member of the
Soulhewn

Biography
Once a cobbler, Iscea was in the
Dreadlands
where she endured splinter-storms for weeks. She eventually succumbed and became a Shardborne, but because of how long she'd been able to resist the corrupting effects, her transformation was left unusually incomplete. The creature now known as "Twofold Rebirth" wore the ravaged body of Iscea like a skin, and wielded the remnants of Iscea's humanity like a weapon, allowing her to control the minds of
humans
with a single glance.
. After her death, her
foot
and
claw
were sealed in the Helliquary.

Helliquary
boss
in
Diablo Immortal
, introduced in the
Splintered Souls
update. She is fought in the
Citadel of Resurgence
.
Phase 1
"Chosen of the shard... yesssss..."
Iscea rises from her throne

: Iscea shoots a claw from one of her tentacles at the player. This is her basic attack for the phase.

to attack.

Vortex
: Iscea creates a vortex on a large area around herself. Initially negligible, the pull increases over time.
Bone Spikes
: After the vortex expires, Iscea summons 2 sets of bone spikes around herself.
This skill does massive damage. It is best avoided by escaping the vortex that precedes it.

======================================================================
PAGE: Issatar
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Issatar
======================================================================

Issatar
was a
beast
that once plagued
Hezerit Valley
with its brood, but later became their protector.
Biography
Issatar was once the most feared amongst the monsters of Hezerit Valley. Each year it prowled longer into the night, passing through shadows to steal pigs and chickens from townsfolk, and string entrails about.
In autumn, the people prepared for Issatar with pitchforks and spears. They found it feeding from their livestock, and stabbed it through the windows of the barn, and wrapped it in chains.
Issatar's brood attacked Hezerit that night. They leapt upon the distracted humans, and their screams coursed through the valley. When the brood found Issatar chained, they mutilated Issatar, and Issatar too screamed.
Issatar's brood had taken innumerable captives into the shadows, none taken had ever returned alive. The people broke Issatar's coiled claws, but did not slay it, and it came to understand mercy.
The humans left to attack Issatar brood. They charged with burning torches, and drove them into the darkness. Issatar though bleeding from its wounds, took a spear up, and stood before the people, and slew its siblings.
After the battle Issatar slumbered in Hezerit, and in the morning the humans swept up the ash and blood. They offered livestock to appease Issatar, and it guarded them with spear and shadow for a hundred years.
At this point, Issatar was old and close to death. It limped from Hezerit with a debt repaid. Its shattered claws were ingrown; its gait halting. Though the people beseeched it to stay, their need had become what animated Issatar. It could not pass on under their gaze. This, too, was mercy.
Legacy
Depictions of Issatar vary in the Hezerit. Some show it in its monstrous prime; others as an avenger, more human than beast. None capture the meager and quiet way it perished, and thus its legend remains.
In-game
Issatar is mentioned in
Diablo Immortal
, in the flavor text of the pieces of
Issatar Imbued
item set
.
Trivia
It was not recorded what exact beast Issatar was. However, from its legends, it was a nocturnal
predator
with clawed hands,
lived in groups of broods,
was capable of intellect
and empathy,
had a life span of more than a century,
was capable of standing upright (at least for a time)
and wield a spear.
References

PAGE: Izel
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Izel
======================================================================

Izel
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Ethnicity
Kehjistani
(presumed)
Class
Artisan
Occupation
Poultice vendor
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Izel
was a poultice vendor based in
Caldeum
.
Biography
From the simplest ingredients, Izel fashioned poultices beloved in Caldeum. They soothed burns and healed scars, but also fostered dependency in those who tried them. She was careful to never sell to the same person twice.
She made powders from what she could cultivate in the desert: cacti and willow she planted with gold flake runoff begged from an alchemist. The costs took all her money, and the growing season was long, but Caldeum was massive, and many were the hurts of the people. The need for her work would never end.
Izel had used her powders for years: when the sun creased her skin, when cacti spines pricked at her, when a filthy cat clawed her at the bazaar. She had discovered the properties of her work firsthand. An artisan forever avails themselves of what they create.
After years of selling just enough to feed herself, word of Izel's skill spread. Caldeum's
Trade Consortium
began to notice, and approached her with simple offers of patronage that would have left her poorer than before. She refused them to a one, and spat on their shadows.
Izel's offer was simple: she would share her work with the Consortium, but only as a ruling member of the council. By the time she returned home, the pact was already complete; a
gold
coin with the likeness of her face lay on her doorstep.
Legbreakers
from the Trade Consortium burned Izel's nursery, ripped up her plants, and spat on the sand. Five of them stole into her shack in the night, found Izel swaddled in heavy covers, and stabbed at her slumbering form.
The attackers'
swords
were tuned aside by shields of light, and their bodies
burned
in golden radiance. Izel rose from her slumber with blazing eyes, swept the ashes from her shack, and returned to sleep.
The Consortium plied Izel more carefully now, leaving pouches full of coins and brilliant topaz outside her house without so much as a whisper of obligation. She gathered her attackers' ashes into a simple wooden box, and left it on the steps of their gathering-house with a note.
In-game
Izel is mentioned in
Diablo Immortal
, in the flavor text of the pieces of
Seeds of Sown Gold
item set
.
References

PAGE: Jentulf
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Jentulf
======================================================================

Jentulf
Title
Royal Apothecary
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Westmarch
Society of Apothecaries
Occupation
Apothecary
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Diablo III
(mentioned only)
Royal Apothecary Jentulf
was a prodigious, eccentric potion maker in service of
Justinian IV
.
Biography
Bounties
As an assistant apothecary of
Westmarch
, in
1270
, Jentulf offered a number of
bounties
to
adventurers
.
Jentulf heard of
the Countess
, and how she had been resurrected in a
blood ritual
. Wishing to learn more about her and her methods, he requested that
adventurers
retrieve some of her
blood
. He was willing to pay well for even a single drop of it.
He also requested that venom be delivered to him from the fangs of
Toxic Lurkers
, promising payment upon delivery.
Going further afield, he requested the hearts of
demons
from the
Molten Egress
. He requested that haste be made in retrieving them, for if he could not find the hearts soon, a recent mistake he made would become permanent.
Royal Apothecary
Later, Jentulf was a leading apothecary at the royal court of
Westmarch
, crafting potions to enhance the
king's
army, as a member of His Majesty's war council.
He did so in a very controversial manner, however
. Apparently, he himself did not fully realize exactly how his potions worked, yet was sure of being the greatest apothecary of his time.
He was known to draw ideas from others sometimes, putting them to effective use.
After making a
potion
that allowed the taking life of the slain for oneself, he promptly tested it by committing murder. Jentulf was put to trial afterwards and sentenced to imprisonment. The apothecary genuinely did not understand what did he do wrong, accusing the judges of being simply jealous.
In prison, stripped of his title, he pleaded the king for early release, promising to create more invigorating potions.
Later, Jentulf was granted freedom and reinstated. However, he became more sinister afterwards, believing that fear is the greatest motivation, which reflected on his new creations.
His contempt towards the other apothecaries grew greatly, as Jentulf believed they all expected him to lose his talent during imprisonment.
In the end, Jentulf disappeared without a trace, stating in his final letter that his genius transcended benevolence and embraced chaos.
In-game
Diablo Immortal
Jentulf is referenced in
Diablo Immortal
, as the provider of the "
Blood of the Countess
, "
Arach Venom
," and "
Molten Hearts
" bounties.
Diablo III
Jentulf is first referenced in
Diablo III
. Here, his
Legendary Potions
can be obtained as in-game items, each of them (except
Bottomless Potion of Kulle-Aid
and
Bottomless Potion of the Unfettered
) telling a part of Jentulf's story.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
The king Jentulf serves goes unnamed in
Diablo III
(not to mention its court and country), but in
Diablo Immortal
, it is strongly implied to be the
King of Westmarch
. Given the timeframe of the game, and how the events described in the
Diablo III
text must come after it, the king he serves has to be Justinian IV.
References

Jered Cain
Gender
Male

Jered Cain
was the son of
Deckard
and
Amelia Cain
.
Biography
Life
Born in
1233
, Jered was named after his father's
famous ancestor
. He had a distant relationship with his father, who was often absent, missing his first words and first steps, and not being there for him when he came down with fever, a condition that nearly killed him.
Jered played with
Gillian
in their youths.
At the age of four, Jered witnessed what would be the final argument between his parents, the same argument that had been repeated throughout his entire life. On the spot, his mother took him with her and headed east from
Tristram
to live with her mother.
They never made it however, as the wagon they were traveling in was attacked. Both Jered and his mother were killed in the robbery.
Thomas Abbey
's
men
suspected that they had been killed by bandits, but the perpetrators were never found.
Legacy
"I grew up with him, don't you remember? Until he disappeared—"
"Enough! Do not speak of that."
-
Gillian
and Cain (not) discussing Jered
(
src
)
Cain shows the portrait of his family to
Karshun
and
the Shard-seeker
The deaths of his wife and son haunted Deckard decades after their death, and he still held onto the death notice he had received concerning them. He kept a portrait of himself with Amelia and an infant Jered, as it was the last thing he had of them, save memories.
Years later
,
Belial
turned Cain's grief against him. Twisting the truth as per his wont as the Lord of Lies, Belial claimed that Jered and his mother were actually attacked by
khazra
, their souls dragged down into the
Burning Hells
to writhe in agony. In the end though, Deckard saw through his lies.

PAGE: Jerhyn

"Greetings, honored traveler. I am Jerhyn, Lord of Lut Gholein, and I bid you welcome to my fair port-city."

Jerhyn
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Lut Gholein
Occupation

Status
Active (as of
1264
)
Appearances
Diablo II
Legacy of Blood
(mentioned only)
To Hell and Back
Jerhyn
was the sultan of
Lut Gholein
.
Biography
Early History
In his youth, Jerhyn purchased minor love potions from
Lysander
, hoping to win the favors of the harem girls. At some point. Jerhyn succeeded his father as sultan of Lut Gholein.
In
1263
, he was visited by
Jazreth
, who was interested in the history of the palace. Jerhyn gave him a tour. When he found ancient seals over a passageway in the cellar, he became very agitated. He asked for some time alone to study them, and Jerhyn granted it. Shortly after, he left with no further word. Jerhyn never saw him again.
The Siege of Lut Gholein
"To any who aid me in the defense of Lut Gholein, I pledge my support. Passage east, wealth, honor - all are due to those who help my city."
- Jerhyn
(
src
)
The
following year
, his city was beset by troubles that began with the coming of the
Dark Wanderer
. His people began whispering of the
dead
rising from their tombs, and
monsters
roaming the dunes of
Aranoch
at night. Jerhyn himself witnessed things that he could not explain. He ordered the port closed and all trade ships moored until he could be sure that his city was safe. When the troubles began here, he allowed the terrified harem guilds to join him within the safety of the palace. All was fine, until one night, screams echoed up the stairwells from the harem. His guards arrived to find the girls being slaughtered by
demons
. The guards were able to push the demons back through the rift from which they'd come from, but the demons kept coming through, and the palace guards were left to fight a losing battle. Jerhyn hired
Greiz
and his mercenaries to protect the city, but knew that matters were growing worse by the hour. Still, he had to choose his confidantes carefuly, lest he send the city into a panic.
Such confidantes came in the form of a
group of heroes
, who were in pursuit of the Dark Wanderer. After witnessing their deeds, he told them of the evil that had beset the palace.
They successfully slew the Summoner (the same
man
that Jerhyn had seen a year ago), ending the threat to the palace.
Impressed with their skills and bravery, he confided that
Drognan
and himself had concluded (correctly) that the Dark Wanderer was
Diablo
himself, that the Lord of Terror sought the
Tomb of Tal Rasha
, in a bid to free
Baal
. The heroes set out in pursuit, but the
Prime Evils
escaped. Jerhyn authorized
Meshif
to take them over the
Twin Seas
to
Kehjistan
, so that their hunt may continue. He gave them his final thanks, and told them they would always be welcome in his city.
In-game
Jerhyn
Appears in
Diablo II
Significance
Medium
Service(s)
gossip, directions,
Quest
initiation
Residence(s)
Lut Gholein
Starts quest(s)

,

Portrayed by
Jim Killeen

Act II
of
Diablo II
. Upon the player's arrival in Lut Gholein, Jerhyn greets them at Warriv's camp. In addition to his introduction and his suggestion to talk to
Atma
, he has a special dialogue option breaking down what services the player can get from which vendor. Jerhyn will subsequently be found at the steps of the palace.

Introduction
General
Greetings, honored traveler, I am Jerhyn, Lord of Lut Gholein, and I bid you welcome to my fair port-city. I'm glad to know that once again caravans are free to travel through the Western Pass.
For some time now, we have been under siege by an evil power that I cannot identify. Strange... It all began when a
Dark Wanderer
came this way, looking for the
Tomb of Tal Rasha
. No one knows exactly where
Tal Rasha
, Keeper of
Baal
, is entombed, but it is certain to be far out in the desert.
Now, my people whisper tales of the dead rising from their tombs and horrible creatures lurking amongst the moonlit dunes. Even I have witnessed things which I cannot explain. I've ordered the port closed and all trade ships moored until I am sure that my city is safe.
Atma
, the tavernkeeper, has an
important mission
for you. Go see her immediately. You'll find her on the other side of town.
Now, I must return to the palace. I apologize, but I can't invite you in. Things are... rather a mess right now.
About the Merchants
Merchants
For trade in magic and the like, see
Drognan
or
Lysander
. Drognan is the wisest man I know - without equal in magic and ancient lore. Poor Lysander is nearly deaf, but he's a reliable potion chemist.
For travel back west, see
Warriv
, whom you already know.
Our own
Fara
is a fine and honest armorer, and she can heal wounds as well.
Elzix
is the innkeeper and may also have some items to trade.
Greiz
, the
mercenary
captain I hired to secure the gates of Lut Gholein, keeps order in town, as well.
There are others here, too. I'm sure you'll meet most of them. Just look around...
Gossip
State of things
Things are getting worse by the hour. I know everything looks fine, but trust me, it isn't!
Lut Gholein
To any who aid me in the defense of Lut Gholein, I pledge my support. Passage East, wealth, honor - all are due to those who help my city.
Confidants
You seem very capable, but no offense is intended when I say that I must choose my confidants carefully. It wouldn't do to have rumors sending everyone into a panic.
Elzix
Even though he was once a bandit, I permitted Elzix to take over the Deseret Rain Inn. He has been quite civilized ever since.
Warriv
When you arrived, Warriv's caravan had been long overdue. With all of the evil that's arisen in the land, I'm surprised he got through at all.
Meshif
Meshif is an honorable man, but I fear that he is growing impatient with me about impounding his ship. I dare not tell him what's really happening in this city.
Atma
The woman, Atma, may have some useful gossip for you. She can always be found near her public house.
Tainted Sun
After initiated
My astrologers failed to predict this eclipse. You should seek Drognan's advice.
Early Return
This eclipse is a definite manifestation of evil.
Upon Completion
The sun again shines on Lut Gholein! I'm beginning to like you, traveler.
Arcane Sanctuary
After Initiated
When the troubles began here, I allowed the terrified Harem guilds to join me within the safety of the palace. All was fine, until one night...
Screams echoed up the stairwells from the harem. My guards arrived to find the poor girls being slaughtered by a merciless band of hell-spawned demons. My brave guardsmen tried to push the demons back into the mysterious rift from which they came.
Ever since, my men have fought a losing battle. Demons have continued to pour through the rift into the palace. Ultimately, I hired Greiz and his mercenaries to help protect the rest of my fair city.
Drognan believes that the
Arcane Sanctuary
lies buried underneath this palace, since Lut Gholein occupies the site of an ancient
Vizjerei
fortress.
My palace is open to you now... Take care.
Early Return
There was an
eastern mage
... a Vizjerei, I believe... who visited me almost a year ago. He was very interested in the history of this site, and he seemed particularly fascinated with the palace architecture.
I gave him a tour. When he found the ancient seals over a passageway in the cellar, he became very agitated. He asked for some time alone to study them, and I granted it.
Shortly after, he left with no further word and I never saw him again. Odd... Don't you think?
Upon Completion
I thank you for your heroic aid! I'm also glad that you found something you were looking for. The journal should help you find the True Tomb of Tal Rasha. Hopefully, there is still time to get there before
Diablo
.
Go now. And good luck.
The Summoner
Early Return
The man you describe is probably not
Horazon
.
He sounds like the very mage who came around here a while ago. He was very curious about this palace and seemed especially interested in the seal on the passageway in the cellar. He left shortly after that. I wonder how he got down there? The seal was never broken...
That mage spoke a great deal to Drognan. Why don't you ask him about it?
Upon Completion
The demonic force that was emanating from the corrupted Sanctuary has dissipated. I thank you greatly for your help. Now, we can look to rebuilding our lives.
All will be for nothing, though, if you do not stop the greater Evil which is rapidly gaining ground.
The Seven Tombs
Quest Initiation
I have heard of your many deeds of skill and bravery. I feel I can trust you with something I have been hesitant to speak of...
Drognan and I have concluded that the Dark Wanderer who passed through here recently was Diablo, himself! Drognan believes that Diablo is searching the desert for the secret tomb where the great Horadric mage, Tal Rasha, keeps Baal imprisoned.
You must find Diablo and put an end to the terrible evil that has fallen upon our city. Drognan is wise and is sure to have some helpful advice for you as to how Tal Rasha's tomb may be found.
It may take you quite some time to find The Tomb. May you be ready when you do.
After Initiated
It is well-known that there are seven great Horadric tombs hidden beneath the sands in the farthest reaches of the desert. One of them surely must be Tal Rasha's prison. You must explore each of the tombs to find Tal Rasha's exact location.
Of course, Diablo is searching for the Tomb as well... No one can guess as to what terrors he has unleashed in his search.
Upon Completion
You have done very well. Few could have come this far, let alone discover the True Tomb of Tal Rasha. Unfortunately, I hear that Diablo and Baal have eluded your grasp. This is most unfortunate...
If you wish to travel East, I have authorized Meshif to give you passage by sea. I imagine he should be very anxious to leave by now.
Good luck on your quest, and thank you again for saving my beloved city. You will always be welcome in Lut Gholein, my friend.
Gossip about Jerhyn
Some of the other locals give their thoughts concerning Jerhyn.
Atma
In addition to my public house, there used to be several brothels doing business here. When the troubles first started in the desert, the harem guilds sought sanctuary within the palace.
Of course, Jerhyn was glad to oblige. I'll bet they're finding many ways to repay him for his protection.
Drognan
When the recent troubles began, Lord Jerhyn came seeking my council. I advised him to close the port and put the town under strict watch.
Lately, though, he's been occupied within the palace. I doubt his whores could divert him from his civic duties for this long, though.
Elzix
We've all fared well under Jerhyn's leadership. The town has remained safe throughout this whole mess; and yet the lad still seems very upset about something.
Elzix
An 'Arcane Sanctuary' under the palace? I'd heard that there were some underground cellar levels that Jerhyn used as chambers for his treasure and such, but no Arcane Sanctuary.
Geglash
Jerhyn's been acting strange lately. I can't imagine why he recalled the town guards into the palace. If there is something wrong in there, I hope he doesn't expect me to handle it.
Greiz
Jerhyn hired me and my mercenaries to help keep the peace around here. We're not cheap, but we're the best this wasteland has to offer.
Greiz
Jerhyn's got a nice little trading post going here. Despite his youth, he is a clever businessman. As you can see by that palace, he's done quite well for himself.
Greiz
We're keeping the town safe and tight, but I've got a hunch there's something Jerhyn's not telling us.
Lysander
Oh... Young Jerhyn used to purchase minor love potions from me, hoping to win the favors of the harem girls.
But now that the girls have taken up residence in the palace, he doesn't come around here anymore. Well, well... I've always said, 'alchemy is no substitute for experience'.
Meshif
There's something Jerhyn's not telling me, I just don't know what. To my eye, things here in town don't look that bad, especially since Warriv's caravan route opened up.
Warriv
Jerhyn has his father's strength and wits. He's young, but he rules this place with wisdom and care. I think he'll grow into a fine Sultan... Provided we all survive this crisis.
Personality and Traits
Jerhyn was a young man during the time of the
Darkening of Tristram
and its aftermath. He has good leadership ability, and he is well liked by his people.
Warriv
believed that he had his father's strength and wits, and in time, would grow into a fine sultan.
Greiz
considered him to be a fine businessman.

Jezran Rasheen
was the only son of a prominent merchant in the city of
Toraja
. The dark-skinned youth had listened well to
Uldyssian
's plea and had chosen to follow him.
Jezran was killed during the assault on the Temple of the
Triune
in Toroja. However, according to
Mendeln
, Jezran did not hold Uldyssian responsible for his demise.

PAGE: Jondo Mouren
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Jondo_Mouren
======================================================================

"Looking for adventure,
traveler
? Use a Crest and delve the mysteries of the
Elder Rift
."
- Jondo Mouren
(
src
)
Jondo Mouren
Title
Crest Merchant
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Occupation
Merchant
Status
Active
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
Jondo Mouren, Crest Merchant
is a merchant of
Westmarch
.
Biography
In
1270
, the royal
Mages
of Westmarch made a breakthrough with the
Elder Rift
in the
capital
. Mouren and other merchants were given permission to sell
crests
to "qualified individuals," granting them access to the Rift. Unfortunately for Jouren, everyone who entered the Rift died inside. This changed with an
hero/group of heroes
, who entered the Rift, survived, and brought back news of the horrors they'd encountered, and useful items they'd found. Overjoyed to hear it, Mouren declared that business would boom once word spread of the treasures that awaited inside the Rift.
In-game
Mouren is a vendor in
Diablo Immortal
. He is found in the
Palace Courtyard
in Westmarch, and is introduced in the
quest
"
Braving the Rift
."
Items sold
Eternal Legendary Crest
for 1600
Platinum
, limit: 1 per week, requires completing a
Helliquary
raid with at least 4 members from the player's
Warband
Eternal Legendary Crest
for 160
Eternal Orbs
Legendary Crest
for 1600
Platinum
, limit: 1 per week
Rare Crest
for 200
Platinum
, limit: 3 per week
History
The Eternal Legendary Crest option after completing a Warband raid was added in the
July 20, 2022
update.
The (bound) Legendary Crest and Rare Crest options were added in the
September 28, 2022
update.

Kael Rills
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Khanduras
Relatives
Unnamed wife
Unnamed children
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo
The Awakening
Kael Rills
was a resident of
Tristram
.
During the
Darkening of Tristram
, he was among the townsfolk who followed
Archbishop Lazarus
into the labyrinth beneath the
Tristram Cathedral
to find
Albrecht
. They were set upon by
the Butcher
. After months of torture, Kael managed to make it to the surface, albeit grieviously wounded. He entreated a
trio
of
heroes
to avenge them, before he succumbed to his wounds.
In-game
Kael appears in
Diablo I
when
"The Butcher"
quest
is available. He is not named in the game itself, and is only referred to as "the Wounded Townsman." After he dies, becomes "The Slain Townsman," and his body remains near the cathedral until the Butcher is killed.
Quotes

Please, listen to me. The archbishop Lazarus, he led us down here to find the lost prince. The bastard led us into a trap! Now everyone is dead... Killed by a demon he called The Butcher. Avenge us! Find this butcher and slay him so that our souls may finally rest...
" (from "The Butcher" quest)
"
Please help....! I barely escaped from....... The Butcher...! He killed.... My wife... My children! I beg of you...... In the name of God......... Avenge them.........
" (from a pre-released demo version of the game)
Trivia

Kael is only named in
The Awakening
RPG supplement. Unlike the PC game, the player(s) have the opportunity to save him if a healing effect is applied quickly enough.

======================================================================
PAGE: Kaelan
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Kaelan
======================================================================

Kaelan
Appears in
Diablo II
Significance
Minor
Service(s)
None
Residence(s)
Lut Gholein
Starts quest(s)
None
Portrayed by
Presumably
Tony Pope
Kaelan
is an NPC guard that stands watch over the palace in
Lut Gholein
. Much like
Flavie
and
Hadriel
, Kaelan serves no purpose aside of guarding an area the player may not yet enter. But unlike the other two, who are more of a warning of impending danger in the tougher areas, the area Kaelan guards cannot be entered by the player without his, or in a more proper sense, Jerhyn's permission after the player has created the
Horadric Staff
and has started the search for the
Arcane Sanctuary
.
Kaelan guards the
Harem
levels and the succeeding
Palace Cellar
levels of the palace in Lut Gholein. He will step aside if the player properly completes the aforementioned chain of quests in
Act II
, at which time the player will be granted access to the area beneath the palace.
Role
Kaelan plays a very minor role in advancing the storyline of Diablo II. He stands guard outside the Palace with a nameless partner and is depicted as one of the
Desert Mercenaries
who can be hired from
Greiz
. He is certainly not a Palace Guard, because the Guard's uniform has much more armor and padding as can be seen from their corpses in the lower levels of the Palace.
Kaelan does not speak much, nor does anyone mention him in their quotes. He has a total of four lines of dialogue - a greeting, which cannot in any form be thought of as a
greeting
and four talking phrases.
Quotes
Before gaining the
Arcane Sanctuary
quest:
"
Halt!!!
" (aforementioned
greeting
when the player gets close to the Palace)
"
You may not pass.
"
After speaking to
Jerhyn
about the Arcane Sanctuary:
"
Stay out of trouble.
" (immediately after the quest is gained, until the player leaves the city in some way)
"
Welcome to the Palace.
"
"
You may enter the Palace
."
Removed:
"Hey, hero. You're asking for trouble if you leave town now."

PAGE: Kala (Diablo III)
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Kala_(Diablo_III)
======================================================================

For the
Barbarian
of the same name, see
Kala (Diablo II)
.
"I have never been outside the city my entire life. I have never even been outside the palace. When they threw us out here, I thought I would die. I was terrified. But now...look at his view. I have never understood how large the
world
actually was. It is beautiful."
- Kala
(
src
)
Kala
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Affiliation
Kehjistan
Occupation
Noble (formerly)
Status
Active
Appearances
Diablo III
Kala
is a former noble of
Caldeum
and aspiring poet.
Biography
Kala grew up inside the
Imperial Palace
. She never ventured outside it.
She dreamed of being a famous poet like
Solan
.
In
1285
, she and numerous other nobles were expelled from the palace at the order of Emperor
Hakan II
. She thought she would die, and was terrified.
She sold everything she owned just to get by.
However, she made her way to a
camp
that overlooked the city from a bluff. She found the view to be beautiful.
She shared her history and poetry with
The Nephalem
.
After Belial's defeat, she thanked The Nephalem for what they had done, and told them that she was leaving. She stated that Caldeum had never been home to her, but had rather been a beautiful prison. Perhaps she would die on the road, but if so, she would do so with the world stretching out before her.
In-game
Kala is an
NPC
in
Act II
of
Diablo III
. She is found in the Hidden Camp. During the "
Betrayer of the Horadrim
"
quest
, she will drop the
Kala's Poem
tome
.
Quotes
I have never been outside the city my entire life. I have never even been outside the palace. When they threw us out here, I thought I would die. I was terrified. But now...look at his view. I have never understood how large the world actually was. It is beautiful.
I stayed outside last night. I tried to ignore the silence, but the empty air felt like an open mouth above my head. Eventually, I realized I had to sleep. If someone was going to kill me, I was already dead. I hadn’t slept that well in years.
A week ago, I was deafened by the voices. Council members argued in the corridors outside my chambers. Guards chanted on their patrols, and scribes murmured incessantly. Out here, there is only the wind.
I was just another highborn courtier in the palace, but I dreamed of being a famous poet like Solan. Have you read his work? It makes your heart sing! My ability is nowhere near his, but I suppose you will see that for yourself. "When the desert sands silence their whispers in the night, and the thousand lights of the stars bleed into the darkness, I will find you in the void. My love will pour from me as words pour from my pen.
I sold everything I own just to get by. I appreciate everything you’ve done for us, but I have to leave. Caldeum was never home to me. It was a beautiful prison. I may die out there on the road, but it will be in the open air with the world stretching out before me.

======================================================================
PAGE: Kalkos
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Kalkos
======================================================================

Kalkos
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Hawksfire
Occupation
Sailor
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Legacy of Blood
Kalkos
was a crew member of the
Hawksfire
.
While sailing from
Gea Kul
to
Lut Gholein
through the
Twin Seas
, a terrible storm struck the vessel. The crew members tried their best to support the ship through the storm, yet, their efforts were not paying off and the ship began to break down. The armor of
Bartuc
, however, determined to reach Lut Gholein decided to act through
Norrec Vizharan
and summoned
demons
to fix the ship. The sailors and passengers on board of the ship were too terrified of what Norrec had unleashed in front of them that they neglected the fact that it saved their lives. That same night, everyone save for Captain
Casco
decided to ride the lifeboats and abandon the ship. Those of them who survived the rising waves were later attacked by a giant squid-like demonic creature which devoured them all but Kalkos, who nonetheless was badly injured.
Kalkos's body was later found by Captain
Jeronnan
, his crew, and a young
Necromancer
known as
Kara Nightshadow
. The dark mage used a spell to communicate with the dead body and figure out who he was and whether he was on board the ship that carried the armor of Bartuc and its presumed thief. Kara's theory proved true as the dead body confirmed witnessing a
Sorcerer
summoning vile demonic creatures. As Kara continued her questioning the spell began to fade which forced Kara, who was now sure that Kalkos has been with the armor, to cast a different spell that allowed her consciousness to personally relive and witness Kalkos' death. Right when her vision of what was happening began to diminish, she realized that a demon—later discovered to be
Xazax
—was present during Kalkos's death and similarly sought to find the armor of Bartuc and the "fool"  wearing it.

PAGE: Klath-Ulna
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Klath-Ulna
======================================================================

Klath-Ulna
Title
The Golden One
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Bear Tribe
Status
Presumed deceased
Appearances
Diablo IV
(mentioned only)
The Toll of Darkness and Light
"There are stories of him, of Klath-Ulna, called the Golden One, though in every tale he is bathed in Crimson, in the
blood
of any who stand against him."
-
Tejal
(
src
)
Klath-Ulna
was a man who lived during the
Zakarum Crusade
, who in turn, waged a war of vengeance against
Zakarum
itself.
Biography
"I am Klath-Ulna of the
Bear Tribe
, my people are the
Children of Bul-Kathos
, and I am the Golden One. I seek a thing of great importance. An iron bell in yon tower. Bring it to me and I will leave, and no harm will come to any here. Refuse me or stand in my way, and I will lay waste to all who live here. Every man and woman, down to the last infant. This I swear."
- Klath-Ulna to the denizens of
Saint's Calling
(
src
)
Klath-Ulna destroys a Zakarum bell
Klath-Ulna first went to war
during the Zakarum Crusade, when Zakarum forces sacked and plundered Klath-Ulna's
village
. Klath-Ulna was the only survivor, and he began a one-man war against the Zakarum in response. He attacked Zakarum-held settlements, defiling their holy symbols and stripping them of their
gold
,
displaying them as beacons of his vengeance.
Of the towns who resisted, he slaughtered them to the last person.
Klath-Ulna also took
weapons
from the towns he attacked, adding them to his arsenal. With every town pillaged, Klath-Ulna's arsenal grew, and they were used as his instruments of revenge.
His suit of armor was constructed from bells taken from Zakarum churches. It is capped with a helmet taken from the church of the town of
Saint's Calling
.
Determined to make the Zakarum pay for their sins, Klath-Ulna was blinded by his own self-righteousness.

stub
. You can help the Diablo Wiki to become more awesome by

======================================================================
PAGE: Kormac
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Kormac
======================================================================

Kormac
Title
The Templar
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Westmarch
(formerly)
Templar Order
(formerly)
The Nephalem
Disciples of Sanctuary
Class
Templar
Status
Active (as of
1286
Appearances
Diablo III
Diablo III: Reaper of Souls
The Art of Diablo III
"I will never succumb to your evil."
- Kormac
(src)
Kormac the Templar
is one of the three
followers
featured in
Diablo III
.
Biography
Recruitment
"I do not know much of your order. Were you born a Templar?"
"No. Our scripture says, "As a farmer reaps his wheat, so must the order harvest and purify the weeds."
"You say you are a weed. I think that even weeds have their purpose under the sun and moon."
"No. They strangle. They corrupt. And the crop fails. I was lucky to be taken when I was."
-
The Nephalem
and Kormac discussing the latter's past
(
src
)
Kormac was once a soldier of
Westmarch
. However, he was conscripted by the
Templar Order
and initiated by force. He was chained to a wall by the order's inquisitors and beaten mercilessly. By the third day, he was mad from pain and hunger. That was when the whipping began. Kormac would later be told that he relived all of his past transgressions, of everything that brought him tainted joy, that the whip took away his joy and sin. By the end of it, he was a loyal follower of the Order, and was unable to remember his "sinful" past.
Over the course of his service, Kormac was regarded as a paragon among them.
The End of Days
New Tristram
"I am Kormac, warrior of the templar order. If it is the Skeleton King you seek, then you will have to fight your way past Jondar. There is no reason we should hunt alone."
- Kormac introduces himself to The Nephalem
(
src
)
Kormac
In
1285
, Kormac was in
Khanduras
. In the
Tristram Cathedral
, he was betrayed by his fellow Templar
Jondar
, incapacitated, and disarmed by
Dark Cultists
. He was soon freed by a group of heroes however, and he was able to rearm. The heroes intended to confront the
Skeleton King
, and Kormac, seeing that their goals aligned, agreed to ally with them. After re-arming, Kormac took his revenge on Jondar, who had thrown in his lot with the
Coven
. The rogue Templar was killed, and in his last moments, Jondar begged for forgiveness. Kormac replied that betrayal could never be forgiven.
After the fight, he took a journal off Jondar's corpse.
Kormac later thanked the heroes for their aid. As they too fought against the minions of
Hell
, he agreed to join them on the condition that he be allowed to keep any sacred tomes of his Order.
The heroes agreed, but commented that Kormac did not seem like the kind of person who was once as sinful as he claimed, and wondered if there was any such 'sin' to be found. Kormac admitted that the idea had indeed occurred to him, but voiced his dismay that if that were true, it would ruin everything he fought for.
Caldeum
By the time the party reached
Caldeum
, Kormac had had much time to reflect on his companions' suggestion. He decided to confront his past. Still, the present had to be confronted as well. A present which involved the enchantress,
Eirena
, joining the group. Kormac was instantly attracted to her, though his vows as a Templar kept his actions in check.
Kormac
Kormac later conversed with his companions over the issue of his past again, telling them of the journal he had taken off Jondar's body. It was written in an ancient Templar cipher, and while it would take time, he could translate it. He reasoned that by studying Jondar's treachery, he could gain insight into his past. He requested, however, that his friends slay him if he lapsed into his old sins. Despite his resolve, Kormac was afraid—Jondar had betrayed the Order, but what if he had discovered something that made him betray himself?
Reading the journal, Kormac ascertained that Jondar had found a set of what he called "key words" hidden in a dusty libram. Apparently, when Jondar read those words, memories from his past returned to torment him. It was at this point that he began to mistrust the Order. Kormac declared himself ready to look upon the same words, but urged his friends to understand that if he died, he would still be loyal to the
Light
. His friends assured him that he was testing his faith, and there was no shame in that.
Kormac proceeded to read the words. Memories came flooding back, allowing him to remember his time as a soldier of Westmarch, that he had been forcefully conscripted into the Order and lied to about his "past sins." Shaken, Kormac nonetheless reasoned that the inquisitors must have acted without the blessing of the Order's grand master, and declared that once he returned with the tomes, the master would punish the inquisitors.
Bastion's Keep
The group's journey led them to
Bastion's Keep
, for a final confrontation with
Azmodan
and his
forces
. By the time of their arrival, Kormac had studied Jondar's journal further. He found a torn page within the binding, which he believed to be from one of the tomes he sought. He considered it strange that Jondar would hide it as such, as if it were proof of a crime. Studying the page, Kormac realized that the writing contained instructions for the creation of
magical
weapons, yet a rune displayed matched one on the armor of
Tyrael
, a former
angel
of
Heaven
. Taking the parchment to Tyrael himself, the former angel explained that the plans were for angelic weapons that would fit
human
hands.
Tyrael reasoned that the manuscript implied that the
Heavenly Host
intended to destroy
Sanctuary
, and the Templar Order had been created to stop them. A claim that once had weight in the last days of the
Sin War
, but was no longer true. Kormac resolved to see things through to the end, but once the battle was over, he would march back to the Order and have justice for their sins and lies.
A Final Betrayal
Kormac and his companions had to endure one last betrayal as
Adria
turned upon them, her actions leading to the death of her daughter
Leah
and the rebirth of
Diablo
as a single
Prime Evil
. Kormac reflected on the history of the Coven, and reasoned that Adria must have once been allied with
Maghda
, and left to find Diablo in
Tristram
over twenty years ago. However, the heroes were able to succeed, defeating Diablo and his forces and saving both Heaven and the mortal realm in the process.
Return to Westmarch
"I dedicated my life to a lie. Everything I thought I knew...it was all in the service to a madman. I swear that every templar I meet will be freed from the lies of the order. And if they refuse, I will be forced to convince them."
- Kormac
(
src
)
Kormac and his companions journeyed to
Westmarch
, only to find his old home under attack by the
Reapers
.
Kormac confronts the Grand Maester
After successfully repelling the invaders and securing the
city
, Kormac decided to pay a visit to the Templar headquarters, the
Vault of the Order
, in order to confront the
Grand Maester
and tell him about the atrocious techniques the Inquisitors were using on recruits (i.e. wiping their memory through torture). However, upon arrival, Kormac found out that the Order was welcoming him as a hero (the greatest templar ever, the one who defeated Belial and Azmodan) and that torture of neophytes was no longer a secret, being performed with consent of the Grand Maester. Furious, Kormac ordered the initiates to be unshackled (the Inquisitor did so, stating that such is the wish of the greatest one in the Order) and faced the Grand Maester, questioning him about how could he ever allow this. The Grand Maester, truly proud of Kormac's accomplishments, replied that such measures were necessary, and offered Kormac to be his second in command and eventually become Grand Maester himself. After Kormac refused, the Templars' leader ordered to kill him and his companions, but was slain along with his guards, and Kormac made a decision to leave the Order for good. He swore that every Templar he met would be freed from the lies of the Order...by force, if necessary. In the meantime, however, he remained sworn to aid the Nephalem.
Disciples of Sanctuary
After long study and observation of The Nephalem, Kormac, Eirena, and Lyndon formed the
Disciples of Sanctuary
, and continued the fight against the minions of Hell.
In-game
Kormac first appears in the quest "
Reign of the Black King
" in
Act I
of
Diablo III
. If the player saves him from the
Dark Cultists
on level 3 of the
Tristram Cathedral
, he will ask the player to help him retrieve his items. He is first named "
Warrior
." Even if the player ignores him and runs right past him, he manages to get free by himself anyway and joins the player, asking them to get his gear.
Even with the chest containing his gear in plain sight he just seems incapable of opening it for himself.
After the player retrieves his items, he will accompany the player through the rest of level 3, culminating in a showdown with his old brother-in-arms
Jondar
, who has become a Necromancer serving the
Dark Coven
. After dispatching him, Kormac will become a follower, able to be selected at will.
The option is given to have him continue accompanying at that point (there is an 80 second countdown: if he is not accepted in that time he returns to town) and he is useful as a tank to defeat the
Skeleton King
. The only downside is that he kills unnecessary enemies which is bad if you want to minimize XP gain to generate a low-level
Leoric's Crown
drop.
If he isn't present when entering Leoric's chamber it won't be possible to go get him since
Town Portal
is disabled upon entry until Leoric's defeated.
Replay
It is possible to replay quests in Act I, but keep Kormac. This includes being able to rescue the Templar, which gives the player two Templars.
This actually leads to unique dialogue. The original templar will say "evil cowers at the sight of just one Templar. Two will bring it to its knees" and refers to the replay-Templar as "brother."
This only lasts until slaying Jondar. At that point a message says he is no longer following you, despite the dialogue saying he agrees to help: he vanishes after breaking the next barrier for you. This means it's not possible to have 2 Templars against the Skeleton King, only the Necromancer.
It makes it very easy to go AFK and just have them kill skeletons, which will be constantly summoned.
Equipment
Kormac's armor progression.
Kormac rushes head first into combat, garbed in heavy armor and brandishing his one-handed weapon and shield. His imposing figure and righteous battle cries inevitably draw the attention of most servants of the
Burning Hells
away from you in battle, though he fights with more of a focus on slaying his foes than on self-preservation. Throughout your journey, Kormac collects
Templar Relics
– chalices, scriptures and fragments of sacred weapons that lend him purpose and power.
Available equipment:
Amulets
Rings
Shields
Daggers
One-handed Axes
One-handed Maces
One-handed Spears
One-handed Swords
Templar Relics
(special item)
Skills
Many of Kormac’s skills focus on improving his capacity as your protector through taunts, new attacks and stuns. When acting in a support role, Kormac can increase party-wide health and resource regeneration, or quickly heal you with a burst of radiance.

Personality and Traits
"That templar you brought to town may seem grim to most, but I think he's hiding a good heart."
- A villager to
The Nephalem
(
src
)
Kormac in full armor
Kormac is a courageous,
headstrong individual, and often rushes into battle with more focus on slaying his foes than self-preservation.
Loyal to the ideals of his Order, in Kormac's words, "love is the surest way to a tragic end," hence why he has forsworn it.
It was an oath that his infatuation with Eirena tested. He likewise came into friction with
Lyndon
, whose personality is the opposite of his own.
After Adria's betrayal and the death of Leah, he was shown to be noticeably agitated, seething with rage over Leah's death and need to kill Adria.
While outwardly grim, Kormac has a good heart, even if he tries to hide it.
Trivia
This section contains facts and trivia relevant to this article.
Kormac is voiced by British actor
Dominic Keating
.

PAGE: Kyla
CATEGORIES: Characters

Kyla
Appears in
Diablo III: Reaper of Souls
Significance
Minor
Service(s)
None
Residence(s)
Captain Haile's House
The Survivors' Enclave
Starts quest(s)
None
Kyla
is a little girl and resident of
Westmarch
.
Despite her age, she valiantly (although to little effect) defended the house she was holed up in and her friend from the
Reapers
. With the aid of
the Nephalem
, they both escaped to
the Survivors' Enclave
. She never returned the sword she "borrowed" from him, though.
She is the daughter of
Hansen Haile
.
In-game
Kyla and her friend in the Enclave
Kyla is found in
Captain Haile's House
during the "
Hide and Seek
"
event
.
After the event has been complete at least once, Kyla can always be found in the Enclave, playing around (directly to the south from
Shen
's cart, where the preaching madman used to be). If approached, she will exclaim "Papa!" happily, or just chat with the small boy (mostly about how awesome she is compared to him). Near the end of the act, Kyla is reunited with her father, who tells the children that the Reapers have been cleared out of Westmarch and will soon be eradicated completely.
Trivia
Kyla's friend initially appears in Bastion's Keep, where he can be spoken to about the death of his parents and his fear of the possible end of the world. After a pep-talk from the player character, he becomes more courageous and vows to become a great hero like the player when he grows up. He'll probably need a different sword, though.

======================================================================
PAGE: Lacthan
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Lacthan
======================================================================

Lacthan
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Margrave
(formerly)
Relatives
Perithan
(brother)
Status
Active
Appearances
Diablo IV
Lacthan
is a former resident of
Margrave
.
Biography
Lacthan lived in Margrave with his brother,
Perithan
. After his brother left with some merchants, some hunters harassed Lacthan, claiming that his brother had set them up, that the merchants Perithan had agreed to lead through a mountain pass had been ambushed at their campsite. As he later explained to
the Wanderer
, while Perithan was not a devout man, he wouldn't have done any such thing, and asked the Wanderer to serve as a bodyguard for him as he explored
Krol Forest
.
They found the campsite, along with the bodies of the merchants, and some of the bandits who'd ambushed them. One of the bandits had scars criss-crossing their forearm, as if made intentionally. To his unease, Lacthan realized that he'd seen similar scars on "unsavory types" who'd met with his brother, and concluded that his brother really had fallen in with the bandits.
The pair headed to the bandits'
hideout
, Lacthan steeling himself to take his brother's life. However, they found Perithan inside the hideout, injured, who explained that no-one was supposed to get hurt in the scheme. That he'd refused to kill and ran, and that the bandits punished him for it. Lacthan believed him, but pointed out that no-one in Margrave would. He told Perithan that they would head south through the smuggler tunnels and start over where no-one knew them. He asked the Wanderer not to tell anyone where they'd gone, and the Wanderer agreed.
In-game
Lacthan is an
NPC
in
Diablo IV
. He can spawn in
Margrave
, west of the pyre. Talking to him initiates the
side quest
"
Bound By Blood
." Lacthan will accompany the player throughout the
quest
.
References

======================================================================
PAGE: Lady Adhelm
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Lady_Adhelm
======================================================================

"We are the shining people; our creed is the wool and torch, our prayer the fire against winter."
- Lady Adhelm
(
src
)
Lady Adhelm
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Affiliation
Olaud's Hutches
Relatives
Big Adhelm
,
Brother Adhelm
,
Little Adhelm
(brothers)
Status
Unknown
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Lady Adhelm
was a member of the Adhelm line and resident of
Olaud's Hutches
.
Biography
The Adhelms stole wool and fur from the dead in Olaud's Hutches, and was cast free to wander, with no provisions and nothing but the clothes on their backs, to expire or to prove their fellow-feeling.
From the first, the wanderers' hunts were meager, and their shivering slowed their limbs and scared the game away. They blamed Lady Adhelm for resting while the others tried and failed. But Lady Adhelm knew that to hunt in weakness was futile, and a single rabbit was not near enough to feed the four of them. She conserved her strength.
At their failure and the Lady's sloth, the wanderers' blood ran hot, and they fell to anger amongst themselves. They shouted and raved, but did not strike with the axes and clubs they had fashioned, and instead marched on, for shedding the
blood
of their kin would mean they would be forever forbidden in the Hutches.
The wanderers came upon a lake, but it was frozen solid, and they could not see the fish below. Their bellies grumbled in unison, and as they stood to leave,
Little Adhelm
did not rise. Lady Adhelm lay Little Adhelm in downy snow, where no trees cast their shadow, and marked him by a cairn of gray stones, and the wanderers vowed to look nevermore upon his body at her behest. When the others slept, she kept watch, and roamed from their camp.
The three remaining Adhelms walked until the glory of an icewall rose before them, and they could travel no further.
Big Adhelm
sunk down in despair, and Lady Adhelm and her
brother
prayed over him, and Lady Adhelm carved signs of him into the ice. But he did not rise, and they turned, and did not stop their wandering. For, as the Lady said, "we are the shining people; our creed is the wool and torch, our prayer the fire against winter."
Now, only Lady and Brother Adhelm remained. They walked, and Brother Adhelm faltered. Brother Adhelm asked his sister why she was still strong, and she replied that her faith kept her strong. At this Brother Adhelm yearned for his faith, and put his head upon the snow to rest, and Lady Adhelm said she would go to seek warmth and food for him, and vanished into the falling sleet.
She staggered along the path where her younger kin had fallen, for she knew the way. At the hidden grave of each, she espied their useless and empty hands. There she looked upon their bitten flesh with revulsion, but with hunger greater still. Per the creed of her people, she consumed the flesh of her kin.
Once she had slaked the terrible emptiness in her belly, Lady Adhelm piled up their clothes, took what remained of their warmth and returned to Olaud's Hutches. "I have proven my fellow-feeling, for I carry my family's warmth to you," she proclaimed. And they welcomed her among them, for warmth in winter was grander than any sin.
References

.

======================================================================
PAGE: Lady Victoria
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Lady_Victoria
======================================================================

Lady Victoria in her human form
Lady Victoria, The Doomed Woman
is a
unique
Succubus
that can be found in
House of Deep Sorrow
in
Diablo III
. She spawns for an unmarked event.
Victoria transformed
Immediately after you enter the House of Deep Sorrow, you'll see her (in her human form) drained of her soul by three
Exorcists
or
Shadows of Death
. They will not attack you until you attack them, so she will shout on you to leave while you still can (which you can do at this point). If you kill the Reapers, Lady Victoria will become interactable. Upon speaking to her, she will say that the
Reapers
stripped her humanity from her, and will transform into a Succubus. She will have Electrified and Fast affixes.
Upon death, she will always leave
The Horrible Secret
book, revealing that her mother survived a demon attack, implying that the attack in question led to Victoria being half-human and half-demon (and thus more demonic than most humans in Sanctuary).

PAGE: Lester
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Lester
======================================================================

The following article contains information from  the
Diablo I
expansion
Hellfire
, which is of ambiguous canon status.
"So you're the hero everyone's been talking about. Perhaps you could help a poor, simple farmer out of a terrible mess? At the edge of my orchard, just south of here, there's a horrible thing swelling out of the ground! I can't get to my crops or my bales of hay, and my poor cows will starve."
- Lester
(
src
)
Lester
Title
The Farmer
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Khanduras
Occupation
Farmer
Appearances
Diablo: Hellfire
Lester the Farmer
was an inhabitant of
Tristram
.
Biography
During the
Darkening of Tristram
, Lester found something swelling out of the ground, preventing him from getting to his crops and bales of hay. After seeing
Adria
, she gave him a
rune bomb
, saying it would remove the thing from the field. He asked a
hero
to do it for him, as he had to watch his
cows
. The hero obliged and detonated the bomb, revealing the entrance to the
Festering Nest
.
In-game
Lester is exclusive to
Diablo: Hellfire
. He can be seen talking to his cows, and the other townsfolk think he has gone mad, but feel sorry for him because he lost everything. He initiates the
Farmer's Orchard
quest. Unlike the classic
Diablo
NPCs, Lester does not have any gossip and can not be asked about quests. After the hero opens up the Hive with the rune bomb, the next time he/she returns to Tristram from underground, Lester will have departed.
In beta versions of
Hellfire
, Lester used to have a bigger role as a comic relief character. Using the
Command.txt exploit
replaces Lester with the
Complete Nut
(Lester in disguise), allowing players to take the
Jersey's Jersey
quest. It's possible that, originally, Lester would remain on the map as Complete Nut rather than disappear after his quests.

arrived, Clyfton, much to his chagrin, single-handedly raised a catapult, while The Nephalem fended off attacking
demons
. With that done, he asked The Nephalem if they could not tell
Captain Haile
that he'd shouted at them, as he'd promised him that he'd watch his temper.
In-game

NPC
encountered in

of
Diablo III
. He is encountered at the end of the
quest
"
Turning the Tide
," where he raises the third and final catapult.

======================================================================
PAGE: Linn
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Linn
======================================================================

"The smaller brown-haired woman was a thrill-seeker, with a sense of joy that would have served her well. She had believed she was worth something, even if the
world
was not."
-
Zebediah
on Linn
(
src
)
Linn
Gender
Female
Race
Human
Occupation
Tailor (or similar)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Instincts
Linn
was a tailor (or similar) based in
Kingsport
.
In addition to her ability to work with silk, Linn had skill in poetry. She weighed seven stone, and had a tiny, apple-shaped face with auburn hair.
Zebediah
considered Linn to be a thrill-seeker with a sense of joy and a sense of self-belief.
Biography
Living in Kingsport and ran a shop in the city's eastern slums. Linn was the friend of
Alodie
. When reflecting on the matter, Alodie couldn't say what brought them together, but knew that Linn's skill in poetry was what kept them together. The two operated as thieves to varying extents. One time, Linn stole rose powder and wax from a tanner. Alodie served as the lookout.
Early in the year of Linn's last year of life, she and Alodie got dead drunk and wrote “ALMS” in cow’s blood on the leather hood of one of the carriages that Alodie served. However, the carriage looked pristine the next morning. Nobody was punished; nobody even mentioned it. Later in the year, Alodie introduced Linn to the family. She praised Linn's talents, and managed to get her a seat at the mercantile table. This resulted in Linn gaining a delivery of silk.
Instincts
"Sard yourself,
pinch-nose
. I hope your mum’s cats eat her eyes and
demons
eat the cats."
- Linn
(
src
)
While Linn had taken the silk in good faith, her business wasn't fast enough to repay the debt she owed. Linn was visited by two enforcers of the family—
Boyce
, and Alodie herself. Alodie tried to play peacemaker, but Boyce wasn't having it. He smashed various jars, and bound Linn. He stuffed a rag in her mouth and picked up a hammer, ready to smash her teeth. Alodie tried to negotiate on Linn's behalf, but while this spared her teeth, Boyce instead used the hammer to break the knuckles of her right hand. Alodie pointed out that this would prevent Linn from paying the family back (working with silk, her hands were necessary), but Boyce was unperturbed. He took Linn out of her shop, telling Alodie that there were other ways she could pay the family back.
To this end, Linn was added to a shipment of
human
cargo which headed into the
Solterwood
via carriage. Due to being a late addition to the delivery, Linn wasn't drugged like the rest of them. Alodie snuck into the carriage transporting Linn, and was able to free her. Linn told Alodie that she and the other prisoners were being taken as bait. At that point, a
vampire
attacked the carriages, but Alodie and Linn were able to escape, fleeing into the Solterwood. Alodie led her, but Linn had to stop numerous times. The two bickered over what had transpired in Kingsport, but were able to make amends.
They continued to head through the wood, coming across a dead
horse
along the way. They headed south until they reached a wall. Alodie led them into a nearby cave, pointing out that it would do them no good to keep walking until they collapsed from exhaustion. However, the vampire followed them into the cave and attacked them, infecting both women with vampirism. They were avenged moments later by
Zebediah
; a
Blood Knight
. Looking at their bodies, as their transformation into
thralls
began, Zebediah knew he had time to only save one of them and chose Alodie. The infection having been stilled, she begged Zebediah to likewise save Linn, but he explained that she was already too far gone. He explained, albeit indirectly, that Linn would not have been able to walk the path of a Blood Knight, whereas Alodie had a chance. Alodie took Linn's ascot as a keepsake before plunging a
spear
into her chest, granting her the peace of
death
.
References

======================================================================
PAGE: Little Adhelm
CATEGORIES: Characters
URL: https://diablo.fandom.com/wiki/Little_Adhelm
======================================================================

Little Adhelm
Gender
Male
Race
Human
Affiliation
Olaud's Hutches
Relatives
Big Adhelm
,
Brother Adhelm
(brothers),
Lady Adhelm
(sister)
Status
Deceased
Appearances
Diablo Immortal
(mentioned only)
Little Adhelm
was a member of the Adhelm line, and resident of
Olaud's Hutches
.
Biography
The Adhelms stole wool and fur from the dead in Olaud's Hutches, and was cast free to wander, with no provisions and nothing but the clothes on their backs, to expire or to prove their fellow-feeling.
From the first, the wanderers' hunts were meager, and their shivering slowed their limbs and scared the game away. They blamed Lady Adhelm for resting while the others tried and failed. But Lady Adhelm knew that to hunt in weakness was futile, and a single rabbit was not near enough to feed the four of them. She conserved her strength.
At their failure and the Lady's sloth, the wanderers' blood ran hot, and they fell to anger amongst themselves. They shouted and raved, but did not strike with the axes and clubs they had fashioned, and instead marched on, for shedding the
blood
of their kin would mean they would be forever forbidden in the Hutches.
The wanderers came upon a lake, but it was frozen solid, and they could not see the fish below. Their bellies grumbled in unison, and as they stood to leave, Little Adhelm did not rise. Lady Adhelm lay Little Adhelm in downy snow, where no trees cast their shadow, and marked him by a cairn of gray stones, and the wanderers vowed to look nevermore upon his body at her behest.
Little Adhelm's flesh was later consumed by his sister
before she returned to Olaud's Hutches.

- Lord Martanos
